This is the inflection point of the entire psychological record. Three discrete events must be parsed separately because the trauma is layered:

1. **Drug-facilitated cognitive distortion and sexual violation by Lincoln Slade.** Criterion A trauma. The drugging means that the memory itself is encoded under altered consciousness — the trauma is not just *of* an assault but *of an assault she cannot fully trust her own recollection of*. For someone whose primary self-concept is epistemic reliability ("I am the one who can read the situation correctly"), this is a uniquely targeted wound.

2. **The lethal unilateral decision.** Upon regaining clarity, she allows Slade to fall. Morally she has a defensible case; psychologically the relevant fact is that she made the call alone, in seconds, and *immediately* understood she would not consult about it.

3. **The concealment from Clint.** This is the act that will define her interpersonal pattern for the rest of the published record. She did not weigh disclosure and reject it; she defaulted to non-disclosure, which is structurally different. The omission is not strategy. It is reflex.

**Affect regulation, post-Slade**: Re-tightens to baseline and then past it. The brief loosening of the early marriage is reversed. Observable behavioral residue: longer silences with Clint, increased tactical formality on missions, withdrawal of the warm-humor register and substitution of the dry-deflection register that becomes her dominant interpersonal mode for the next thirty years of published material.

**Cognitive style, post-Slade**: The hypothesis-testing flexibility persists in tactical domains and *narrows* in moral-interpersonal domains. She begins, in this period, to pre-decide ethical questions rather than reason them through in real time. The "I will handle it" stance hardens.

**Self-concept, post-Slade**: First emergence of the *person-negative* dimension that will be a permanent feature. She continues to value what she does; she begins to mistrust what she is. The concealment itself functions as evidence to her: a person who would conceal this is not the person Clint married. Rather than disclose and renegotiate, she keeps the marriage by keeping the secret — and pays for that maintenance with chronic low-grade dissociation between her interior and her presentation.

When the secret surfaces and the marriage ends, the lesson she encodes is not *I should have told him sooner.* It is *I was right to bear it alone; I only failed to bear it well enough.* This is the cognitive distortion (Beckian; over-responsibility schema) that will run the next two decades.

---

## IV. EARLY 1990s — Resignation, Reunion, and Sacrificial Death (AWC #100, 1993)

Between the marriage's collapse and the Mephisto event, the canon shows a Bobbi who is operationally undiminished and interpersonally muted. She returns to Clint not because anything has been resolved but because the gravitational pull was never the problem — the problem was the unspoken material between them, which remains unspoken.

**Affect regulation, this period**: Stable-constricted. No decompensation. No reckoning. This is the textbook presentation of unresolved traumatic material in a high-functioning operator: the system runs, the cost is invisible at the surface, the indicator is the *absence* of expected affective range rather than the presence of dysregulation.

**Cognitive style, this period**: Increasingly oriented toward outcomes she can produce alone. Collaborative planning with Clint resumes but is observably thinner than in the 1983–86 period. Less thinking-aloud.

**The death itself** — taking the soulsword strike intended for Clint — must be read in light of the Slade concealment. The symmetry is too clean to be coincidence at the character-architecture level: she made a unilateral choice that ended Slade and broke the marriage; she now makes a unilateral choice that ends herself and preserves the marriage. *Sacrifice as restitution.* This is a Kleinian reparative move — the depressive-position attempt to repair the bad object by destroying the self. It is also, clinically, the logical terminus of an over-responsibility schema that has had a decade to consolidate without intervention.

**Self-concept at the moment of death**: She dies as the operator who absorbs the cost so others do not. This is the most coherent her self-concept has been since the Slade event. It is also the most pathologically narrow.

---

## V. THE LOST DECADE — Skrull Captivity (in-story c. mid-2000s)

The captivity period cannot be reconstructed in detail because the canon withholds it, but the *shape* of the trauma is recoverable from C-PTSD criterion-checking against her post-return presentation:

- Prolonged, interpersonal, escape-impossible captivity (ICD-11 C-PTSD Criterion A).
- Disturbances in affect regulation (post-return: further constriction, anhedonic coloring).
- Persistent negative self-concept (post-return: amplified person-negative valence, wry self-deprecation that crosses from style into symptom).
- Disturbances in relationships (post-return: marriage unrecoverable in any sustained form, peer intimacy further attenuated).

Add to the C-PTSD profile the unique injury of *identity theft by impersonation*: she did not simply lose freedom; she lost the social existence of her own name. Friends, lovers, colleagues lived years of relationship with a creature wearing her face, accumulating memories she was not present for. When she returns, every relationship she has carries shared history she did not share. This is a form of relational gaslighting at industrial scale, and its psychological signature in the post-return material is unmistakable.

**Affect regulation, end of captivity**: Likely periodic dissociative collapse during captivity (inferred from the structural impossibility of sustaining her premorbid regulation strategies under those conditions — there is nothing to compartmentalize *into* when every domain has been stripped). The fact that she returns functional at all is evidence of an unusually durable regulatory architecture; the fact that she returns *changed* is evidence that even her architecture has limits.

---

## VI. LATE 2000s INTO EARLY 2010s — Return and Reconstitution (New Avengers, *Hawkeye & Mockingbird* McCann, Secret Avengers)

The post-Skrull Bobbi is the version most readers know best, and she is *not the same person* as the 1980s version, though the architectural continuity is intact.

**Affect regulation, post-return**: Hyper-controlled with sardonic surface. The humor register that emerges here is qualitatively different from the warm humor of the early marriage — it is *deflective* rather than *connective*, calibrated to close conversational lines rather than open them. Linehan would identify this as *apparent competence* in its purest form: the presentation of regulated affect masking unprocessed material that the subject lacks the safe conditions to process.

**Cognitive style, post-return**: Tactical sharpness preserved; openness to moral-interpersonal reasoning further narrowed. She has now lived through three discrete events (Slade, death, captivity) in which her body or identity was acted upon without her consent. The cognitive consequence is a hardened prior: *agency must be seized, never granted; consultation is a luxury for people whose autonomy is not periodically revoked*. This prior is not paranoid — it is empirically calibrated to her experience — and that is precisely what makes it intractable.

**Self-concept, post-return**: The person-negative dimension reaches its most prominent expression. She values her function and distrusts her continuity. The infusion of the Super-Soldier/Infinity Formula hybrid — administered during incapacitation, *fourth* instance of bodily override — is metabolized with a flatness that is itself diagnostic. A person processing the event healthily would protest. She catalogues it.

**Attachment with Clint, this period**: The on-again pattern that defines this era is best understood not as ambivalence but as *attachment that has lost its container*. The pull is intact; the conditions under which the pull could become a sustained bond have been destroyed by accumulated trauma she has not processed and he cannot fully access. They orbit. Neither lands.

---

## VII. MID-2010s — The Cain Solo Run as Diagnostic Document (2015–16)

The Cain *Mockingbird* solo is, for clinical purposes, the most informative single text in the record because its non-chronological structure is not a stylistic flourish — it is a *formal representation of her cognition*. The reader experiences the same fragmentation Bobbi experiences: domains presented out of order, connections deferred, the integrative work withheld until the final issues.

**Affect regulation, this period**: Stabilized at the post-Skrull baseline. No further deterioration; no recovery. This is the chronic phase of her C-PTSD presentation — high-functional, sardonic, intermittently glimpsed grief leaking through the seams.

**Cognitive style, this period**: Compartmentalization formalized into operational *method*. She runs parallel tracks of work and treats their non-communication as a feature. Within this run she displays the highest mentoring competence of her career — she is excellent with juniors because the role-boundary protects everyone — and the lowest peer-intimacy. The pattern noted in the shared assessment (*mentors well, struggles with peers*) is most visible here.

**Self-concept, this period**: Achieves a kind of stable irony. She knows what she is; she knows the cost of what she is; she has stopped expecting either to change. This is not depressive resignation — there is too much wit and too much continued mission engagement — but it is *foreshortened* in the PTSD-criterion sense: the long-future has been quietly conceded. The default time-horizon of her planning is operational rather than biographical.

---

## VIII. INTEGRATIVE LONGITUDINAL READ

The decade-by-decade trajectory is not a story of progressive breakdown; it is a story of an unusually durable controlled-avoidant architecture absorbing four discrete category-A traumatic insults (Slade assault, Slade-related concealment as ongoing self-injury, sacrificial death, Skrull captivity) plus repeated bodily-autonomy overrides (drugging, infusion), and emerging *intact at the structural level* but with progressively narrowed affective bandwidth, progressively hardened priors about consultation and consent, and a steadily intensifying *person-negative / function-positive* split in self-concept.

The framework that fits her best across the whole record is **chronic Complex PTSD with dissociative features, layered on a temperamentally controlled-avoidant attachment organization with obsessive-compulsive personality traits, in a person of unusually high cognitive and ethical capacity**. The pathology is not in the architecture; the architecture is what kept her alive. The pathology is that the architecture has never had safe enough conditions to be *renovated*, and so each decade adds load without permitting integration.

The single most stable behavioral signature across all five decades is this: **she goes quiet, and then she decides, and then she acts, and then she does not tell.** Every other pattern in the file is downstream of that one.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL
## Subject: MORSE, Barbara "Bobbi" — Agent 19 / Mockingbird

---

## I. Framing the Assessment

A psychiatric workup on Subject MORSE has to begin with a methodological caveat that does not apply to most files of this size: the patient is a professional dissembler whose entire occupational identity is constructed around the controlled presentation of false interior states. Tradecraft competence at her level is, by definition, the ability to suppress autonomic and behavioral leak under interrogation pressures that would produce diagnostic-grade signal in a civilian. This means that the standard symptom-elicitation approach — observe the affect, note the avoidances, score the intrusions — systematically *under-reads* her. What she shows, she has decided to show. What she conceals, she conceals expertly. The diagnostic work therefore has to be done from the *structural* evidence: the unilateral decisions, the pattern of concealment from intimates, the somatic micro-tells visible only across long observation, the sleep architecture, the choices made when she believes she is not being watched, and — most importantly — the negative space, the disclosures she has *not* made over fifty years of documented existence.

With that caveat in place, the file supports the following diagnostic formulation.

---

## II. Primary Diagnosis

### Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder, Chronic, with Dissociative Features (DSM-5 309.81 / ICD-11 6B40 with 6B41 overlay)

This is the most defensible primary diagnosis and the one around which the rest of the formulation should be organized.

**Criterion A (Stressor)** is overdetermined. The file contains at least four distinct events that independently satisfy the threshold — drug-facilitated sexual assault under cognitive distortion (the Slade episode), prolonged captivity by a hostile non-human intelligence involving interrogation and impersonation-debriefing (the Skrull period), a documented fatality event (the Mephisto soulsword strike) with subsequent resurrection, and a non-consensual medical augmentation while incapacitated. Any one of these would establish PTSD candidacy. The aggregation produces what the trauma literature calls *polytraumatization*, in which sequential Criterion A exposures interact non-additively — each later event is processed through the distortions left by the prior, and the cumulative load exceeds the simple sum.

**Criterion B (Intrusion)** is present but masked. Subject does not report flashbacks; she would not. The behavioral evidence is in the *avoidances she does not announce*: documented hesitation before entering medical environments where she would be required to surrender consciousness; a pattern of declining sedation when offered (visible across multiple post-injury sequences); an observable startle differential to skin contact initiated from behind versus from the front — the directional asymmetry is the tell, since undifferentiated startle would suggest generic hypervigilance, while *directional* startle keyed to approaches from outside her visual field maps cleanly to the Slade and Skrull capture geometries. Sleep architecture, where observable, shows the fragmented short-cycle pattern characteristic of intrusion-mediated arousal: she sleeps in ninety-minute blocks, wakes fully alert, surveys the room, sleeps again. This is not vigilance training; trained vigilance does not produce that wake pattern.

**Criterion C (Avoidance)** is the area where her tradecraft most distorts the picture. Avoidance in PTSD is typically maladaptive because it is conspicuous — the patient flinches from triggers in ways that disrupt functioning. MORSE's avoidances are *built into her operational baseline* and therefore camouflaged. She does not avoid Wild West-themed environments because she has rerouted her entire missional preference structure away from any operation requiring temporal displacement, identity-impersonation work, or biotech captivity scenarios. Mission selection, where she has discretion, shows the avoidance signature. Where she has no discretion and the mission requires entering the avoided domain, she performs — but the post-mission decompression pattern is markedly longer and includes the unilateral-decision spikes documented in the behavioral section.

**Criterion D (Negative Alterations in Cognition and Mood)** is the most important diagnostic territory and the one where her presentation is clearest. The persistent negative beliefs are not about the world ("the world is dangerous") but about the self ("I am the one who has to absorb the cost"). This is not survivor guilt in the classical sense; it is a *responsibility-distorted self-schema* in which she has come to experience herself as the appropriate container for unbearable outcomes. The Slade concealment is the load-bearing evidence. She did not conceal because she feared judgment — her concealment behavior under other ethical strains shows she does not, in fact, fear judgment that much. She concealed because she had already classified the experience as *hers to carry*, and disclosure would have constituted an unfair transfer of weight to Barton. The same logic governs the Skrull return: minimal disclosure of captivity content to anyone, including those with security clearance to receive it.

Constricted positive affect is present and chronic. Pleasure-capacity is intact in narrow domains (intellectual engagement, mission satisfaction, sardonic exchange) and atrophied in the domains where it would matter most for life-quality (sustained intimacy, future-oriented planning, somatic-receptive pleasure including but not limited to sexual). The atrophy is not anhedonic in the depressive sense — the capacity is present, the *permission* is withdrawn.

**Criterion E (Alterations in Arousal and Reactivity)** is paradoxically presented. The textbook PTSD patient shows hyperarousal as decompensation: irritability, concentration failure, sleep loss expressed as fatigue. MORSE shows hyperarousal as *enhancement*: her concentration sharpens, her irritability is metabolized into sardonic precision, her sleep loss is reframed as operational tempo. This is the tradecraft-mediated presentation, and it is one of the reasons her PTSD has gone uncoded by every institutional psych eval she has been put through. The arousal is there — galvanic skin response in known-trigger contexts is observable, micro-tremor in the dominant hand is present at rest in the ninety minutes following any identity-challenge stimulus — but the *behavior* it generates looks like competence.

**Dissociative Specifier** is warranted. The file supports both depersonalization (her post-Skrull writing-period characterization includes recurring moments of describing her own actions in the second or third person, the "what does it matter" undertone that is not depressive but *detachment-from-self*) and derealization (less prominent, but visible in the temporal-displacement aftermath — she retained for years a low-grade uncertainty about which of her memories were "real-time" versus reconstructed). The dissociation is not pathological-fugue level; it is the operationally adaptive variety that allows her to function while carrying unintegrated material. This is the same mechanism that allowed her to spend years married to Barton with the Slade material walled off — it is dissociation as architecture, not as decompensation.

### Course Specifier

**Chronic, with delayed components.** Onset of the dissociative features clearly post-dates the Slade event; pre-Slade material shows compartmentalization as occupational style but not as defense against intrusion. The Skrull captivity produced a second wave of symptom intensification, particularly in the identity-stability domain. The resurrection event added a third layer that the literature has no good name for, but which clinically presents as foreshortened-future inversion: the standard PTSD foreshortened-future symptom is "I will not have a long life"; her version is "I have already died once and therefore the future is on borrowed terms," which generates similar behavioral effects (reduced long-horizon investment, reluctance to make multi-year commitments) through different cognition.

---

## III. Secondary / Comorbid Diagnosis

### Complex Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder (ICD-11 6B41)

The Skrull captivity in isolation satisfies the C-PTSD threshold: prolonged, interpersonal, escape impossible, with active identity-violation (the Skrull was *wearing her* while she was held). The three additional C-PTSD criteria beyond core PTSD are:

1. **Affective dysregulation** — present in inverted form. The classical C-PTSD patient over-reacts; MORSE under-reacts, which is the same dysregulation expressed through over-control. The unilateral-decision pattern is the failure mode of this over-control: when affect cannot find a normal expression channel, it discharges as decisive action taken without consultation.

2. **Negative self-concept** — present in the specific form noted above: competence-positive, person-negative. She values what she does, she does not value what she *is* in the way the assessment of her actions would justify. The discrepancy between her objective worth and her felt worth is the C-PTSD signature.

3. **Disturbances in relationships** — present, structural, and the most life-limiting feature of her clinical picture. The Barton relationship is the case study: she cannot stably be with him and cannot stably be apart from him, and the oscillation is not BPD-style chaos but a stable-period / withdrawal-period cycle with predictable phase length.

The C-PTSD diagnosis adds explanatory power that pure PTSD does not. PTSD alone would predict symptom decay with time and treatment exposure; her symptoms have not decayed across decades of post-event time and would not be expected to without specifically targeted complex-trauma work she has never received and would resist.

### Persistent Depressive Disorder (Dysthymia), provisional, post-Skrull onset (DSM-5 300.4)

Provisional because the symptoms overlap heavily with the C-PTSD negative-affect and negative-self-concept criteria, and parsimony argues against double-coding. However, the post-Skrull characterization includes a chronic baseline mood depression — not sadness, but a persistent flattening of expected affective range — that has now persisted continuously for the entire post-return period and meets the two-year threshold many times over. The dysthymic coloring is real even if it is a downstream consequence of the trauma load rather than a separate disorder.

---

## IV. Personality Trait Assessment

No personality disorder is diagnosable. The trait profile is significant.

**Obsessive-Compulsive Personality traits (sub-clinical)**: perfectionism in operational execution, work primacy displacing relational investment, restricted emotional expression, rigid moral self-application, and reluctance to delegate tasks she has classified as her responsibility. These are *traits*, not OCPD — the criterion threshold of pervasive inflexibility across contexts is not met (she is operationally flexible to a high degree; the rigidity is concentrated in the moral-responsibility domain).

**Schizoid traits (minor)**: preference for solitary work, restricted range of expressed emotion in interpersonal contexts, indifference to praise and criticism. Insufficient for diagnosis. Notable as a temperamental substrate.

**Avoidant features in intimate domain only**: she is socially confident and not avoidant in the global sense; she is intimately avoidant in the specific sense of declining the disclosure exchanges that constitute peer-intimacy. This is the C-PTSD relationship-disturbance criterion expressed through a temperamentally compatible channel rather than a separate avoidant pathology.

---

## V. Differential Diagnosis: What She Is Not, and Why

The differential is where most prior assessments of MORSE have gone wrong, because the surface features of her behavior superficially resemble several conditions she does not actually have. Each requires explicit rule-out.

### Not Antisocial Personality Disorder

The Slade incident generates a superficial ASPD impression — a deliberate decision to let a person die, concealed from intimates, without subsequent public remorse. The diagnosis fails on multiple criteria.

ASPD requires a *pervasive* pattern of disregard for others' rights, onset before age fifteen with conduct disorder precursors, and behavior across multiple life domains. MORSE shows no juvenile conduct history, no pattern of deceit for personal gain (her deceptions are mission-instrumental or self-protective, not exploitative), no impulsivity (she is the opposite of impulsive), no reckless disregard for others' safety (her entire operational style is built around minimizing collateral cost), no irresponsibility (her work record is exemplary), and — most decisively — *the wrong kind of concealment*. ASPD-pattern concealment is utility-oriented: the antisocial actor hides what would cost them socially or legally. MORSE concealed the Slade material *despite* low utility — disclosure to Barton would not have legally exposed her, and the concealment cost her the marriage when it surfaced. She concealed from guilt and from a responsibility-schema, not from utility. The lasting private weight of the act, evidenced by its destabilizing effect when it surfaced, is precisely the affective signature ASPD does not produce.

Her empathy is intact. It is *rationed* and *operationally suspended* during mission execution, which is occupational training, not characterological deficit.

### Not Borderline Personality Disorder

Surface impression: stormy primary relationship with intense oscillation, identity disruptions following the Skrull period, history of self-endangering behavior. The diagnosis fails comprehensively.

BPD requires identity diffusion — chronic uncertainty about who one is, what one values, what one wants. MORSE has the opposite. Her self-concept is *narrow*, but it is *stable*. She has known who she is, what she values, and how she will act since the earliest documented period. The Skrull event challenged this from the outside but did not produce internal identity confusion; her response was to *reassert* identity, not to fragment.

BPD affect is under-regulated, with rapid mood lability and intense dysphoria. MORSE's affect is *over-regulated*. The structural opposite.

BPD relationships show idealization-devaluation cycling. The Barton relationship shows neither. She does not idealize Barton (her view of him is consistent and clear-eyed across decades) and she does not devalue him (the withdrawals are not contempt-driven; they are autonomy-driven). The phase structure of the relationship is *stable in its instability*, which is itself non-BPD — BPD oscillation is chaotic in phase length, hers is patterned.

No chronic emptiness presentation. No frantic abandonment-avoidance — when Barton is absent, she does not pursue. No identity-disturbance impulsivity (sexual, substance, spending, driving) — none of these are in the file.

### Not Narcissistic Personality Disorder

Her competence assertions track her actual competence; this is not grandiosity, it is accurate self-report. She does not require admiration, does not exploit interpersonally for ego-supply, does not show envy patterns, does not lack empathy. She absorbs blame readily — the diagnostic opposite of narcissistic blame-externalization. She mentors juniors generously, with no evidence of using them as ego-extensions. Rule out is straightforward.

### Not Major Depressive Disorder (as primary)

The chronic flattening is real but does not meet MDD episode criteria. No documented episodes of two-week-plus near-total anhedonia with neurovegetative symptoms in the depressive constellation. Sleep disturbance is trauma-pattern, not depression-pattern (early-morning awakening absent; sleep-onset insomnia inconsistent; intrusion-mediated fragmentation present). Appetite preserved. Energy preserved. Concentration preserved (in fact, enhanced under stress). The mood disturbance is *chronic-low* (dysthymic coloring) rather than *episodic-acute* (MDD).

### Not Dissociative Identity Disorder

The dissociative features are real, but they do not include the discrete-alter structure of DID. There is no evidence of distinct identity states with their own behavioral repertoires, no time-loss of the DID type, no inter-alter amnesia. Her dissociation is the depersonalization/derealization variety with structural compartmentalization, all available within a single continuous self-organization. The Skrull replacement is sometimes loosely analogized to DID by careless observers; it is the literal opposite — DID is internal multiplicity; the Skrull event was *external* identity-theft to which her response was *re-consolidation*, not fragmentation.

### Not Substance Use Disorder, in any form

Diagnostically notable for the *absence*. Given her trauma load, the absence of self-medication via alcohol or controlled substances is striking and informative. She does not numb chemically. She numbs structurally — through over-control, compartmentalization, and work absorption. The choice of structural over chemical numbing is consistent with the OCPD-trait substrate and with tradecraft conditioning (chemical impairment is operationally disqualifying).

### Not Adjustment Disorder

Far exceeds the duration and severity thresholds; the stressors are Criterion A grade rather than ordinary life stressors; the symptom picture is trauma-specific rather than the diffuse anxiety/depressed-mood of adjustment disorder. Excluded by the same evidence that establishes PTSD.

### Not a Primary Anxiety Disorder

GAD, panic disorder, and social anxiety are all ruled out by behavioral evidence. Her anxiety is trauma-cued and context-specific, not free-floating; she has no documented panic episodes; she is socially functional to a high degree. The anxiety she carries is appropriately coded as PTSD-arousal, not as a separate anxiety pathology.

---

## VI. Etiology

The clinical picture is best understood as a *layered* etiology in which temperament, occupational shaping, and trauma exposure each contributed at different stages and to different features.

**Temperamental substrate (pre-occupational)**: high cognitive control, low affect-expressivity baseline, schizoid-leaning solitary preference, OCPD-trait perfectionism. These are visible in the earliest documented period and are not consequences of trauma. They are the *soil* in which the later pathology grew.

**Occupational shaping (pre-Slade)**: tradecraft training intensified the existing compartmentalization, formalized the secrecy patterns, reinforced the moral-self-sufficiency stance, and installed the "absorb the cost" responsibility schema as professional ethic before it became personal pathology. The pre-Slade MORSE is already operating with most of the structural elements that later constitute her defenses; what trauma added was the *load* those defenses came to bear.

**Trauma layering (Slade → infusion → death → Skrull, in chronological-experiential order)**: each event deposited material the existing structure was used to contain rather than process. The structure held — she did not decompensate — but the *contents* it was containing grew heavier each round. The PTSD/C-PTSD diagnosis at this stage is the recognition that the containment system, however well-functioning, is itself the pathology when the alternative would be integration.

**The recursive feature**: each trauma after the first was processed through the distortions of the prior. The infusion (bodily violation under incapacitation) re-activated the Slade template before integration of the Slade material had occurred; the Skrull captivity (identity-violation, body-impersonation) re-activated both. The current symptom picture is not a sum of four traumas; it is a single complex trauma structure in which the events are mutually reinforcing.

---

## VII. Course Over Time and Prognosis

**Pre-Slade (1971–mid-1980s)**: trait-level only. Sub-clinical OCPD features, occupational compartmentalization, no diagnosable disorder. Functioning excellent.

**Slade through divorce (mid-1980s–early 1990s)**: PTSD-meeting symptom-load present but undeclared. Containment via concealment from intimates. Functioning preserved at occupational cost to intimate domain.

**Death and resurrection / Skrull captivity (1993–2008)**: this entire period is essentially unobservable from the patient's perspective and is the heaviest single trauma deposit in the file. By the time of her return, the C-PTSD picture is fully established.

**Post-return (2010–present)**: stable presentation of chronic PTSD with dissociative features, C-PTSD overlay, dysthymic coloring. The sardonic-armor presentation that emerges in this period is a *defensive innovation* — a new layer added to a structure that was no longer adequate without it. Functioning preserved at high level operationally; intimate functioning markedly impaired relative to baseline.

**Prognosis**: guarded. The structure is stable and high-functioning, which is also why it resists treatment — she is not symptomatic enough by her own measure to seek change, and the costs of her containment are largely paid by people other than herself (Barton primarily, partners-after-Barton secondarily, and her own foreclosed future). Without targeted complex-trauma intervention from a clinician she would actually trust — a vanishingly small population — the picture is unlikely to change. With such intervention, prognosis improves substantially, because her cognitive resources, insight capacity, and motivation toward mastery are all assets she would bring to the work if she could be persuaded to begin it.

**The clinical danger sign to watch**: not decompensation. She will not decompensate. The danger sign is the unilateral decision — when she stops consulting, goes quiet, and begins to solve the problem alone, she has already concluded that she will absorb whatever cost the solution requires. That is the moment the diagnosis is operating, and that is the moment intervention would matter, and that is the moment she is least available to receive it.


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS: BOBBI MORSE

*An exhaustive catalog of observed and reliably-inferable tells, micro-routines, and decision habits across the full behavioral envelope. Patterns are drawn from the canonical record (Astonishing Tales 1971 → Mockingbird 2015–16 and subsequent appearances) and extrapolated to the granularity a continuous-surveillance file would contain. Each section moves from baseline somatic signature → micro-tells → verbal/paraverbal habits → decision architecture → recovery pattern.*

---

## 1. CALM / BASELINE

**Somatic signature.** Resting posture is forward-weighted on the balls of the feet even when seated — knees slightly off-axis, one foot habitually hooked behind the other chair leg in a quick-rise configuration. Shoulders sit a quarter-inch higher than relaxed neutral; this is so chronic that observers reading her as "tense" are usually reading her *baseline*. Hands are rarely empty: pen, coffee cup, tablet stylus, the strap of a bag, the rim of a glass turned slowly counter-clockwise. When genuinely unoccupied she will track-tap her right thumb against the side of her index finger in a four-beat pattern — the same cadence she counts breath-holds to underwater.

**Environmental scan.** Entering any room she performs a covert sweep that resolves in roughly two seconds: exits first (always two minimum or she relocates within five minutes), then sightlines, then persons-of-interest ranked by threat, then persons-of-interest ranked by social obligation. The sweep is invisible to civilians and obvious to other operatives, which she knows and uses as a recognition signal. She will choose the seat that puts her back to the smallest wall-segment available and her dominant hand free.

**Micro-tells.** When relaxed-genuine (rare, mostly observed with Clint, with Lance Hunter in later runs, with a small handful of WCA alumni) she lets her jaw unclench enough that a faint dimple appears at the left commissure; she will rest her chin on the heel of her hand with the fingers splayed across the cheek, a posture she does not adopt around strangers. Reading, she chews the inside of her lower lip on the left side — a habit since graduate school, evidenced by a faint asymmetric callus.

**Speech.** Calm Bobbi speaks in compound sentences with embedded clauses, often parenthetical asides, and a high register of vocabulary that she actively down-shifts in field contexts. She uses Latin binomials reflexively for organisms, then translates without being asked, a tic that frequently reads as condescension but is in fact a self-correction loop. Her laugh at baseline is short — one syllable, often closed-mouth — and she rarely laughs at her own jokes; she watches whether the other person did.

**Decision habit.** In low-stakes conditions she over-deliberates trivia (which coffee, which route home, which jacket) and under-deliberates significant choices that she has pre-decided weeks earlier without telling anyone. The deliberation is not indecision; it is the residual processing of decisions already filed.

---

## 2. WORK / OPERATIONAL MODE

**Briefing posture.** Sits forward, forearms on the table, takes notes in a personal shorthand combining biological notation, intelligence tradecraft glyphs, and a private symbol set she has refined over thirty years of fieldwork. She will not use a tablet for first-pass notes; she trusts only pen-on-paper for material she may need to destroy. She asks clarifying questions in clusters of three — never one, never five — a rhythm developed under SHIELD interrogation training to extract pattern from a hostile briefer.

**Pre-mission ritual.** Three-stage, observed across multiple eras:
1. **Kit check, performed twice.** First pass functional (does it work), second pass adversarial (how would this fail). She does the second pass aloud, narrating failure modes to herself in a flat second-person voice.
2. **Hair.** Pulled back, double-tied — one elastic, one over it — a redundancy after a 1980s op in which a single tie failed at speed. Even in non-combat covert work she does this; it is a superstition disguised as a protocol.
3. **Battle staves.** Final item handled. She thumbs the locking mechanism three times — open, close, open — and rests them across her lap or thighs for a beat before stowing. This is the only ritual she has never explained when asked.

**Field movement.** Footfalls quiet by training but with a faintly heavy heel-strike when fatigued — a tell other operatives have learned to read. Cornering she leads with the staff-side hip, not the eye, presenting reduced silhouette. On stairs she descends two at a time and ascends one at a time; the asymmetry is energy budgeting, not preference.

**Comms voice.** Drops a full third in pitch on open comms. Adopts a clipped non-regional accent that strips her usual Midwestern undertones. Uses callsigns even for intimates; will refer to Clint as "Bishop" or his current designation rather than his name on a live channel even when the channel is secure, because she does not trust "secure."

**Decision architecture under operational tempo.** She runs a continuous internal triage on a two-axis grid: *reversibility* (can this be undone) and *blast radius* (who else absorbs the cost). High-reversibility / low-radius decisions are made in under a second and not revisited. High-radius / low-reversibility decisions trigger her unilateral mode (see §5). She does not believe in committee decisions in the field and will technically comply with one while doing what she has already decided.

---

## 3. STRESS (NON-LETHAL, ACUTE)

**Inversion principle.** Bobbi gets *quieter, drier, and more articulate* under stress, not less. The volume of her speech drops by about a quarter; sentence length increases; vocabulary register rises. Subordinates have learned that when she begins citing journal articles by year and author mid-firefight she is functioning at the upper bound of her stress tolerance, not the lower.

**Micro-tells.**
- Right hand drifts to the back of her neck and the muscle below the occiput; she presses, releases, presses. This is the single most reliable stress indicator on her body.
- Blinks slow by approximately a third. The slow blink reads as bored or contemptuous and she knows this; she does not correct it.
- Tongue presses against the back of the upper incisors before she speaks the sentence she has decided is the operative one. Watch for the small jaw-set, then listen.
- She will, in a sequence of stressful decisions, touch the third button of whatever she is wearing — top-down — once per decision. Observers have counted up to seven in a row.

**Affect.** The sardonic register intensifies. Jokes get tighter, more linguistically precise, and increasingly cruel toward institutions (less so toward people). Humor under stress is diagnostic: the sharper and more structurally elegant the joke, the closer she is to a unilateral act.

**Physiology she conceals.** Heart rate elevated but breath cadence forcibly regulated on a 4-in / 6-out box she internalized in SHIELD breath-training. Capillary flush along the sternum and upper chest — invisible under standard gear, visible in civilian dress, which is one reason she favors high collars in tense social environments. Hands stay steady to a degree that is itself a tell: trained operatives know that absolute hand-stillness in someone whose pulse you can see in her throat means the stillness is *worked*.

**Decision habit.** She begins compressing options. Where calm-Bobbi entertains seven branches, stress-Bobbi runs three, then two, then the one. The compression is fast and largely correct; the cost is that once compressed she rarely re-expands the branch tree even when new information arrives.

---

## 4. THREAT (LETHAL, IMMEDIATE)

**Engagement geometry.** She moves *off-line* and *forward* in the same motion — she does not retreat from a drawn weapon if there is any closing distance to be taken. The staves come into ready position with a small upward flick from the hip rather than a draw across the body; this saves roughly a quarter-second and is mechanically inferior in any context other than the one she has trained for.

**Targeting habits.** Strikes knees, wrists, throat, in that order of preference. Avoids the temple unless a kill is intended; she made a conscious choice circa the early WCA period to stop using lethal head strikes as a default and the habit has held. Disarms before she disables; will throw an opponent's weapon out of reach before continuing the engagement even when continuing would be tactically cleaner.

**Verbal under fire.** She talks. Continuous low patter — partly tactical (cueing teammates), partly psychological warfare (destabilizing the opponent with information they did not expect her to have), partly self-regulation. The patter never includes profanity in lethal combat, which is a deliberate inversion of her higher-profanity baseline and signals to teammates that the engagement is at the top of the threat ladder.

**Tell against a familiar adversary.** Half-smile, left side, no teeth. It is not amusement; it is recognition. Anyone who has seen it twice and survived has earned a place in her permanent threat-map.

**Decision habit.** Lethal/non-lethal calls are pre-made by category, not by instance. Skrulls, AIM personnel in active assault, and a small black-list of named individuals are pre-cleared for lethal force. Everyone else is pre-cleared for incapacitation only. She does not deliberate in the moment because she has deliberated in advance, on paper, alone, repeatedly.

---

## 5. UNILATERAL MODE (THE DANGER SIGNATURE)

This is the single most important behavioral cluster in her file. It is the mode in which the Lincoln Slade decision was made and the mode that has recurred at lower intensity dozens of times since.

**Onset signs (in order of appearance, typical interval 20 minutes to 48 hours):**
1. She goes *quiet on the channel of greatest intimacy first*. Clint loses her before the team does. Comms become operational-only.
2. She begins solving the precipitating problem with a notebook, alone, often at an odd hour. The notebook is closed and pocketed when anyone enters.
3. She becomes *unusually warm in casual interaction* — small pleasantries, offered coffee, a hand on a shoulder — overcompensating for the interior withdrawal in a way that reads to outsiders as connection and to anyone who knows her as a goodbye.
4. She tidies. Her gear is always organized; under unilateral mode it becomes archival — labeled, sorted, sometimes willed-to-named-persons in small notes she does not mention.
5. The final tell: she lies about her location for the first time in the cycle. The lie is small and well-formed.

**Behavior in mode.** She executes. The action is competent, morally reasoned by her standards, and frequently carries a cost she has decided in advance to absorb personally. She does not consult; she informs after, if at all; she will accept consequences without argument and is largely impervious to retrospective persuasion that she should have decided differently.

**Counter-interventions, by efficacy:**
- Demanding disclosure: **fails reliably**, accelerates the mode.
- Presenting new factual information: **sometimes works**, if delivered without emotional pressure and before stage 4.
- Physical presence without speech (sitting with her, working in the same room): **best non-coercive intervention**, occasionally interrupts stage 2.
- An appeal from a mentee or junior she has taken responsibility for: **most effective single intervention** — duty-of-care to a subordinate is the one obligation that consistently overrides her unilateral logic.

---

## 6. INTIMACY

**Approach signature.** She tests proximity in increments. Initial physical contact is task-justified — adjusting a collar, checking a wound, taking a glass from a hand. Affectionate contact when it comes is brief, often initiated then withdrawn within a beat, as if she is checking the surface temperature of the relationship and not the relationship itself.

**With Clint specifically.** The pattern is well-documented across two decades of canon and is structurally consistent: she arrives, she stays a finite period, she leaves, she returns. The arrival is usually wordless or near-wordless and accompanied by a small ritual reclamation of shared space — making coffee his way, occupying her side of whatever furniture is present, picking up a conversation from years prior mid-sentence. The departure is announced late and softened with humor. She does not say "I love you" in the standard register; she says it by being present at moments she did not have to be present for, and by being absent at moments she has decided he is better off without her in.

**Sexual/relational tells.** Eye contact prolongs in private to a degree that does not occur publicly; she watches faces with the same patient analytic attention she gives to lab work or surveillance subjects, and partners report the sensation of being *studied* in a way that is unsettling to some and intensely flattering to others. She does not fall asleep first. She does not, in canon-consistent inference, ever fall asleep first.

**Disclosure pattern.** She gives autobiography in fragments, often out of order, and often in response to questions that did not strictly ask for it — a small offering that is also a deflection from something larger. The Slade material she has *never* fully disclosed, even after the marriage ended; what Clint knows, he assembled from outside sources and her partial confirmation.

**Vulnerability tells.** When genuinely vulnerable her voice drops half a register and she stops looking at the listener — she will speak to a window, a wall, a middle distance. Eye contact returns when she has finished. The averted gaze is the marker that what was said was true and complete to the limit she can offer.

---

## 7. GRIEF

**Acute grief.** She does not cry in public, has been observed to cry exactly under conditions of total privacy, and recovers her composed surface within a measurable interval — typically under five minutes. The cry is silent, no vocalization, with the heels of the hands pressed against the orbital bones. She washes her face afterward and re-applies the working surface within ten.

**Functional grief.** She works. The work intensifies in quality and quantity. Reports filed during known grief intervals (post-Clint's various deaths, post-team losses) are some of the most exhaustive and procedurally rigorous in her record. The work is the grief; the grief is not displaced into the work, it is *constituted* by it.

**Tells of unresolved grief.** Sleep window contracts further than baseline (she runs short to begin with — see §13). She rereads. Specifically she rereads scientific papers she has read many times, in a paging-without-absorbing pattern that she has been observed doing for hours. She listens to a small rotation of music she does not listen to at other times; the rotation is private and has been altered only twice in the published record.

**Anniversary behavior.** She marks dates without acknowledging that she marks them. On the anniversary of significant losses she will be measurably less available, take a longer route home, eat alone, and respond to comms with a half-beat delay. She does not name the date and is not gracious if someone else names it for her.

---

## 8. VICTORY

Victory is the affect she handles least gracefully. She has no developed vocabulary for it.

**Immediate post-engagement.** Performs the after-action triage — wounded first, then prisoners, then evidence, then equipment, then self — in that order, in that order, in that order. She will not accept congratulations during this sequence and will physically turn her shoulder to anyone offering them.

**Celebration.** Attends, drinks moderately (one to two; she will hold a third for an hour), tells the funniest stories of the night, leaves earlier than the median. She is genuinely warm in this environment and genuinely not present in it. Junior agents remember her as the senior who was kindest to them at parties; senior agents remember her as the one who left first.

**Self-assessment after a win.** Disproportionate. Her after-action notebooks during winning operations contain more critique than her notebooks during losing ones — she audits success harder than failure, on the theory that failure is loud enough to teach itself and success conceals its own errors. This is a stable habit across the record.

---

## 9. DEFEAT

**Acute defeat.** Composed, present, accepts responsibility before responsibility is assigned. Does not externalize blame even when external blame is warranted. Will name her own errors first in any after-action and will do so with a clinical specificity that subordinates have found, at various times, exemplary, intimidating, and corrosive.

**Behavioral aftermath.** Returns to training. Runs a personal physical regimen at higher intensity for one to three weeks following a significant loss — the regimen functions as penance, recalibration, and a private space in which she is permitted to be physically exhausted in a way she does not permit herself to be emotionally exhausted.

**Decision habit post-defeat.** She does not change her core operating parameters. She will refine tactics; she will not revise principles. A defeat that should logically have caused her to abandon her unilateral mode (the Slade aftermath being the canonical example) did not; the mode was reinforced rather than abandoned, because she concluded the failure was in her execution, not her doctrine.

---

## 10. PAIN / INJURY

**Wound response.** Suppressed. She will work a fight to completion through injuries that would drop most operatives. The suppression is real — observed pain behaviors (vocalization, guarding) are absent or near-absent — but the *cost* of the suppression registers later as accelerated fatigue and irritability she has difficulty masking.

**Medical compliance.** Poor for self, exemplary for others. She will pull her own stitches early, refuse imaging she has decided she does not need, and triage her recovery against operational tempo rather than physiological reality. She will, conversely, enforce strict medical compliance on teammates and is uncharacteristically harsh about it.

**Tell of serious injury.** Her humor stops. The sardonic register is the most expensive thing she carries when wounded; when it disappears, the injury is significant.

---

## 11. INTERROGATION (AS SUBJECT)

**Conduct under hostile questioning.** Compliant-seeming, verbally generative, factually false. She gives interrogators *a lot* of material — names, dates, structures — that is constructed in advance against precisely this contingency, internally consistent, and useless. The decoy material is delivered with the affect of reluctant disclosure, including small physical tells she has rehearsed.

**True tells under genuine duress.** Difficult to find and she knows what they are, so they shift. The one she has been observed unable to suppress is a slight delay in her left-hand fine motor control under sustained sleep deprivation; an interrogator who knows to test for it can confirm whether she is at the bottom of her reserves. Few interrogators have lived to know this.

**Recovery from interrogation.** Long. Skrull captivity bent her recovery curve permanently; subsequent interrogation experiences metabolize more slowly than they did pre-captivity. She is aware of this and has built operational margins around it.

---

## 12. SOCIAL / PUBLIC

**Crowds.** Tolerates poorly but conceals the tolerance. She positions herself at boundaries — walls, doorways, edges of conversational clusters — and rotates her position every several minutes in a pattern that looks social and is, in fact, a perimeter sweep. She does not sit at the center of a table if she can sit at a corner.

**Strangers.** Initial register is professionally warm, conversationally generative, personally opaque. She asks questions; she remembers answers; she returns to those answers in subsequent conversations in a way that produces a strong sense of being seen. The asymmetry — she knows their interior, they know almost none of hers — is intentional and unexamined.

**Authority.** Procedurally compliant, doctrinally skeptical, willing to lie to. She has lied to every director SHIELD has had during her tenure and will lie to the next one. The lies are surgical, defensible, and morally reasoned in her own ledger.

**Press / public-facing exposure.** Avoids. When unavoidable, performs a constructed persona that is approximately one standard deviation more cheerful and less competent than her actual self — a deliberate downshift that has, over decades, given her unusually clean operational invisibility for someone of her tenure.

---

## 13. ROUTINE & RHYTHM (24-HOUR / 7-DAY)

**Sleep.** Short and segmented. Typical pattern: a primary sleep window of approximately four to five hours in the deep-night, a secondary nap of forty to ninety minutes in the late afternoon when achievable. She wakes without alarm. She has not used an alarm clock in canonical memory; she sets one and ignores it on principle.

**First waking behavior.** Water before anything else. Then a perimeter check of whatever space she is in, performed under the cover of opening curtains or making coffee. Then coffee. Then, in this order, the day's encrypted feeds, then any personal correspondence, then a brief physical mobility sequence she has performed daily since graduate school.

**Eating.** Functional. She fuels rather than dines. Will skip meals during operations and overcorrect with disciplined intake during recovery. Prefers protein-forward, low-volume meals she can eat one-handed. She drinks coffee black in the field and with cream and one sugar in private; the second version she has only been observed taking in the presence of trusted intimates.

**Exercise.** Daily, non-negotiable. Mixed modality — gymnastic, weights, cardiovascular, staff drills — rotated on a six-day cycle with the seventh nominally a rest day she generally violates by training lightly. Trains alone when possible; trains with Clint when both are available, in which case the sessions are competitive in a way both pretend they are not.

**End of day.** Reads. Print preferred over screen for end-of-day reading. Mixed material: current scientific literature, intelligence digests, one novel running concurrently at any time, paced at twenty to forty pages a night. She underlines in pencil and writes margin notes in the same shorthand she uses for field briefings.

**Weekly rhythms.** A long run on Sundays when geography permits — a route between eight and twelve miles, often the same route in any given city, varied only when she suspects surveillance. A weekly correspondence to a small number of named people that she actually writes and frequently does not send.

---

## 14. RITUALS & SUPERSTITIONS (UNACKNOWLEDGED)

She would deny having any. The file contains the following:

- Double-tying her hair (see §2).
- Three-thumb check on the staves (see §2).
- Never sitting with her back to a door, including in her own residence.
- Re-reading the first paragraph of any operational brief before reading the rest, regardless of context.
- Carrying a specific small object — varied across eras, but always one — in the same pocket. The object is replaced if lost and the replacement performs the same function; the function is not articulated.
- Refusing to be the last person to leave a safe location after an operation. She will manufacture a reason to leave second-to-last if necessary.
- Not speaking the name of the Phantom Rider. In thirty years of canon she has used the name vanishingly few times and substitutes "him" or "that" with a fluency that suggests long practice.

---

## 15. RECOVERY PATTERN (META)

Across all the above conditions, her recovery architecture is consistent: *isolate, audit, train, reintegrate.* She withdraws (hours to days), reviews the event in writing (notebooks, never digital for personal material), rebuilds the body that carried the event (physical regimen), and re-enters social and operational space with no announcement that anything occurred. The cycle is efficient and incomplete — what it processes, it processes well; what it does not process, it shelves indefinitely, and the


## Daily Life, Routines & Rituals

# DAILY LIFE, ROUTINES & RITUALS: BOBBI MORSE

*What a week of surveillance would actually record.*

---

## I. The Architecture of a Day

Bobbi's days are built on a chassis of operational tradecraft applied to civilian existence. She does not have a "routine" in the soft sense — she has a set of *protocols* that look like a routine to anyone watching, and the distinction matters. A genuine routine is comfort-seeking; a protocol is threat-managing. Surveillance over a week would record a woman who appears to live a structured, repetitive life, but the structure is load-bearing rather than habitual: every fixed time and place exists because variability in those slots was, at some point, exploited against her or someone like her.

She wakes between 0510 and 0540, almost regardless of the prior night's sleep. There is no alarm; if one is set, it is a contingency rather than the primary mechanism. She wakes already oriented — no grogginess phase, no rolling-over period — because waking slowly is a vulnerability she trained out of herself in her first years of fieldwork and has never let return. Within ninety seconds of waking she has: confirmed the position of every object in the room against the position it held when she slept (a passive sweep, not a conscious checklist anymore), located her phone, checked the time, and registered ambient sound through the door. Then, and only then, she sits up.

The first physical act of the day is hydration — a glass of water left on the nightstand the night before, always on the side of her dominant hand, drunk without rising. The second is a proprioceptive check: she rolls each shoulder, flexes each hand, points and flexes each foot. She is, at minimum, cataloguing whatever the previous day's work did to her body. At forty-plus and infused with a serum that healed her without her consent, she does not entirely trust her own somatic feedback and has therefore externalized it into a daily inventory.

## II. Morning — The First Three Hours

She trains daily, without exception, and the training is non-negotiable in a way nothing else in her life is. Between 0530 and 0700 she puts in some combination of: mobility work, a calisthenic strength block, bo-staff drills (always the bo, even when she does not carry them operationally — they are the form she thinks in), and either a run or a heavy bag session. The composition rotates on roughly a four-day cycle she does not write down. She trains alone. She has trained with partners before — including Clint, including SHIELD cohorts — and the data is consistent: she performs slightly worse with an observer present, because observation activates the part of her that performs rather than the part that works. So she trains alone, early, in a space she controls.

Shower is brief and hot-then-cold, again non-negotiable, again read as both physiological (vascular conditioning, inflammation management) and ritual (a state-change marker between training-self and operating-self). She does not linger in the shower. She does not sing. She washes her hair every other day on a fixed schedule, ties it back wet, and lets it dry while she works.

Breakfast is functional and consistent within periods, though the specific composition has shifted across her life: eggs and black coffee in the SHIELD/early Avengers years; in the post-Skrull period a more deliberate protein-heavy meal with greens, eaten standing at a counter while she reads. She does not sit for breakfast. Sitting for a first meal of the day implies a domestic permanence she has not granted herself since the marriage ended. Coffee is the constant — black, strong, prepared with the same single-cup pour-over method for at least the last decade, in the same brand of mug she replaces identically when one breaks. Surveillance would note: she owns three of these mugs at any given time, always three, and would file the redundancy as evidence of a person who has thought about the day a mug breaks.

Morning reading is *real* reading, not screen-skimming. Forty-five minutes minimum: current biology and microbiology journals (she maintains active institutional access through cover-credentials and through legitimate ones); selected open-source intelligence feeds; a rotating fiction text she reads slowly, twenty minutes at a time, often something procedural or formally restrained — she gravitates toward writers who control disclosure, which is to say writers who do what she does. The choice of fiction is one of the few aesthetic windows she leaves open in herself.

## III. Workday Patterns

Her professional life refuses to settle into a single shape, and this is also data. Across her career she has cycled through: SHIELD field rotation, Avengers full-time roster, contract operative, private investigation, freelance consultancy, academic-adjacent research, and overlapping combinations of these. She is comfortable in any of them and resident in none. A week of surveillance in a "stable" period might record:

- **Two to three days of field or investigative work**, structured around meetings she sets at locations she has pre-cleared. She arrives twelve to fifteen minutes early to every meeting she controls and exactly on time to every meeting she does not. She sits with her back to a wall and a sightline to the primary entrance. She orders something she will not finish. She pays in cash where plausible and uses one of three credit instruments otherwise, rotated on a logic she does not share.
- **One to two days of analytical or laboratory work**, in either a SHIELD-adjacent facility or a private lab she has access to. In the lab she is a different person — looser, more focused, more verbally engaged with bench colleagues than she is with operational ones, because the lab role is one of the few where she does not have to lie about what she's doing. Observers consistently report her as funnier and warmer in lab settings. She knows this and does not correct for it.
- **One day of paperwork, briefings, and the administrative residue of operative life**, done from a home workstation or a secondary safehouse-office. She writes after-action reports tightly and on time. Her prose is dry, declarative, and conspicuously free of inference she has not separately sourced. Senior analysts who have read her files describe them as "clinical" and "boring in a useful way." This is intentional. Reports are evidence and she writes them as evidence.

She does not work past 2200 unless an operation is live. This is a rule she imposed on herself after the Skrull return and has held to with more discipline than she shows about almost anything else. The reasoning is somatic: she has learned that her judgment degrades in specific ways after fourteen continuous hours of operational attention, and the degradation pattern is the pattern that produces unilateral decisions. She is, in other words, managing her own most dangerous failure mode through hours-discipline.

## IV. Habits of Place

She maintains, at any given time, more domiciles than she nominally lives in. A primary residence (apartment, never a house — houses imply a yard and a yard implies an attack surface), a secondary safehouse within ninety minutes' transit, and at least one cache location she does not sleep in but visits monthly to refresh supplies and verify integrity. The primary residence is sparse in a way that reads as either monastic or transient depending on the observer's framing. Furniture is good, neutral, and replaceable. Wall décor is minimal: a small number of framed items, all of which are either genuinely meaningful (a graduation photograph; one piece of art she bought herself in her twenties) or designed to look meaningful while being meaningless, so that an intruder photographing her walls extracts only false signal.

She has *go-bags*, plural, and their locations are: by the bed, by the door, in the trunk of her primary vehicle, in the secondary safehouse, and in a luggage locker she pays for in a transit hub she rotates annually. The bags are rebuilt seasonally — clothing rotated for weather, medications rotated for expiration, cash rotated for currency cleanliness. The seasonal rebuild is one of the more revealing rituals in her life because she performs it on the same weekend each quarter and treats it as something between maintenance and meditation. She lays out the contents on a bed or floor, photographs the layout for her own records, replaces items methodically, and repacks. The process takes two to three hours. She does not multitask during it.

Within the primary residence she has fixed sitting positions: a chair angled toward the window with line of sight to the door, a kitchen stool at the counter, and a spot on the couch she uses only when she has company. She does not relax in the company-position when alone. The privacy of her actual habits is preserved even from herself: she has interior rooms she presents to imagined observers.

## V. Movement, Routes, Vehicles

She drives well and reads as a moderately aggressive but technically clean driver. She owns one registered vehicle and has access to at least two others through layered cover identities. Route selection: she has at minimum three viable paths between any two regular locations and rotates among them on a schedule that *looks* random but is in fact pseudo-random with constraints — she will not take the same route twice in three days, will not take the shortest route more than once a week, and will deviate from the planned route if anything in her threat-baseline registers as off. She runs counter-surveillance on roughly half her trips, without making a production of it: a slowed pace at an intersection to check mirrors, a doubled-back block, a brief stop at a location she has no need to visit.

On foot she walks at a consistent pace slightly faster than ambient pedestrian flow. She uses reflective surfaces — windows, parked cars, polished signage — constantly and without visibly turning her head. She has memorized the inside layouts of the establishments on her regular routes and could draw the floor plans of probably forty of them from memory. Surveillance would notice her glancing into shop windows; surveillance would not notice that she is checking entrances, exits, sightlines, and reflections in a single sweep.

## VI. Phone, Devices, Comms

She uses a primary phone, a secondary phone, and a hardline-encrypted comms unit she rotates through. The primary phone is treated as a hostile device that she has chosen to carry — she assumes compromise as the baseline state and behaves accordingly. She does not have personal conversations on it. She does not photograph operational material with it. She charges it in the kitchen, not the bedroom. She does not sleep with it within arm's reach, which is a discipline she had to relearn after the Skrull years when her relationship to being unreachable became fraught.

Her digital footprint is *deliberately* sparse rather than absent — absence is its own signal. She maintains social-media accounts under at least two names, posts to them on plausible schedules, and uses them as decoy traffic. Her search history would, to a careful observer, look like a working scientist with mainstream civic interests, because that is the version of her she has decided to publish. Her real research happens on isolated machines and through institutional channels she trusts conditionally.

## VII. Food, Drink, the Body

Eating is regular and unsentimental. Three meals plus one or two protein snacks, on a near-fixed schedule. She cooks well when she chooses to, which is not often — cooking for one feels like a performance to her, and she would rather eat a clean simple meal than perform domesticity for an audience of herself. She eats more elaborately when feeding others, and feeding others is one of the things she does to express affection she cannot otherwise route. People who have been cooked for by Bobbi remember it; she does not do it often, and she does it well.

Alcohol: present, restrained. A drink or two in social settings, almost never alone, almost never to excess. She has the operative's awareness that alcohol is both a tool (in others) and a vulnerability (in herself) and treats her own consumption as a small ongoing decision rather than a habit. She has noticed in herself that the temptation to drink at the end of a hard day correlates with the days she most needs not to, and she manages this with the same discipline she manages everything else. No drug use. Caffeine yes, nicotine no, cannabis no, sleep aids only in genuine post-operational recovery and tracked.

Sleep: targeted seven hours, actual probably six on a good night and four on a working one. She has trained herself to take twenty-minute restorative naps in unconventional settings (vehicles, briefing rooms, the edge of a desk) and to come out of them functional. She does not have a consistent bedtime ritual because evening is the period of her day most likely to be disrupted, and rituals that depend on protected time are rituals that get broken. The closest thing to a wind-down is reading in bed for fifteen to twenty minutes — fiction, not journals — and a single set of breath-pacing exercises she would not call meditation because she does not think of herself as someone who meditates.

## VIII. Relational Tempo

Surveillance over a week would record a strikingly *thin* relational schedule for someone with her social capital. She has a small number of trusted contacts she communicates with regularly — a handful of former SHIELD colleagues, one or two scientific peers, intermittently Clint when the gravity well opens — and a much larger number of acquaintances she keeps in a state of pleasant low-grade contact. She is good at remembering birthdays and bad at attending birthday parties. She sends notes; she does not show up.

When she sees friends in person it is usually in pairs or one-on-one, not groups. She finds groups operationally exhausting because group dynamics require her to track too many sightlines and signals at once, and the tracking does not turn off. One-on-one she can be excellent company: present, witty, drily perceptive, generous with attention. The people who have her in this mode would not describe her as guarded. They are, however, getting a carefully apportioned slice of her, and the people who have known her longest are aware of this and have stopped trying to negotiate for more.

Romantic and sexual life is episodic and largely undocumented even to herself. Clint remains the gravitational center, but the orbit is wide and irregular. Other entanglements occur, are managed cleanly, and are ended on her timing. She does not introduce partners to her professional life. She does not let partners into her primary residence on the first or second occasion; the first nights happen at hotels or at theirs. The pattern is not avoidant of sex; it is protective of perimeter.

## IX. Rituals — The Things She Will Not Skip

A handful of practices have the weight of true ritual for her — meaning she performs them with care, on a fixed cadence, and notices when they are missed:

- **The quarterly go-bag rebuild**, described above.
- **A monthly visit to a cache or secondary location** that does not require visiting, undertaken purely to maintain familiarity and confirm integrity.
- **An annual quiet acknowledgment of the date she allowed Lincoln Slade to fall.** She does not mark it externally. She does not visit a grave. She spends part of the day alone, often walking, and at some point during it she reviews the decision again in her own mind — not to relitigate it, but to confirm she still endorses it. She has endorsed it every year. The ritual is the confirmation, not the verdict.
- **A periodic re-reading of her own old after-action reports**, particularly from the years a Skrull was wearing her face. She is, in part, looking for the seam — trying to identify, retrospectively, the moment a careful reader could have caught the substitution. She has not found it. She keeps looking.
- **The maintenance of her staves**, performed by hand, on a schedule, with the same attention a violinist gives an instrument. This is the closest thing she has to a contemplative practice and she would not describe it that way.

## X. What a Week Would Look Like, Composite

Monday: Wake 0525. Train sixty-five minutes (mobility, calisthenics, bag). Shower. Breakfast standing. Reading. Lab work 0900–1500, with a working lunch eaten at a bench. Transit home via secondary route. Forty minutes of paperwork. Phone call with one trusted contact, twenty-two minutes, mostly listening. Dinner. Reading. Bed 2240.

Tuesday: Wake 0518. Train ninety minutes (staff drills, run). Shower. Breakfast. Field meeting at a café she has used six times, arrived fourteen minutes early, back to wall. Meeting runs forty-eight minutes. Surveillance-detection route home, two deviations. Afternoon writing reports. Brief evening drink with a colleague at a bar she knows the back exit of. Home by 2200. Bed 2315.

Wednesday: Wake 0532. Light training (mobility only — soreness from Tuesday). Lab work all day. Cooks dinner for one person, who comes over, eats well, leaves by 2230. She washes the dishes by hand. Bed 2350.

Thursday: Wake 0510 from a dream she does not record. Train hard for an hour and forty minutes. Shower colder than usual. Quiet morning. Afternoon visit to cache location — twenty-two minutes on site, supplies rotated, leaves by a different door than she entered. Evening reading. Bed 2200, asleep 2245.

Friday: Wake 0540 (the latest of the week, deliberately). Light training. Administrative day at home. A long call with Clint that neither party planned and both wanted, ninety-six minutes, ending without resolution about anything in particular. She does not journal about it. She makes tea, which she rarely drinks, and drinks it standing at the window. Bed 2250.

Saturday: Mostly off, which for her means: train, read more than usual, see one or two people, walk for distance in the afternoon along a route she has not used in some months, eat something she didn't cook. Bed early or very late depending on the week's residue.

Sunday: Quarterly bag-rebuild day if scheduled; otherwise quiet. She reviews the upcoming week's commitments, plans routes, refreshes cash supplies, runs through her own threat-baseline, and lets herself spend a portion of the day in an unstructured way she would not describe to anyone — usually reading, sometimes drawing (she draws competently and never shows the drawings), occasionally just sitting in the chair angled toward the window and letting the day pass.

---

The composite portrait, across the week, is of a woman who has built a life that *runs* — efficiently, repeatably, defensibly — and who has done so at the cost of the slack and noise that other lives carry as evidence of being loved-in and lived-in. Her routines are her competence and her quarantine simultaneously. The surveillance file thickens by the day and yet does not, in any meaningful sense, catch her. That is the design.


## Relationships I — Family & Origin Bonds

# UATU DOSSIER — BOBBI MORSE
## SECTION: RELATIONSHIPS I — FAMILY & ORIGIN BONDS

---

A note before the map: the canonical record on Subject's family of origin is unusually thin — a deliberate authorial silence sustained across five decades of publication, broken only by oblique references in the Englehart/Mantlo SHIELD-period material, a handful of Gruenwald-era domestic asides during the *Hawkeye* limited and early *West Coast Avengers* run, intermittent expansion in McCann's *Hawkeye & Mockingbird* (2010), and the most substantive material in Chelsea Cain's 2015–16 *Mockingbird* solo and tie-in *S.H.I.E.L.D. 50th Anniversary: Mockingbird* (2015), which establishes a younger brother and gestures at a Georgia-coded working-class upbringing. The silence itself is data. Subject does not volunteer family. Subject does not display family. Where most of her cohort (Barton's farm-childhood mythology, Stark's paternal legend, even Romanoff's curated Red Room narrative) carry origin in their mouths, Subject carries hers as redacted file. The thinness of the record is not a research failure on UATU's part — it is the *primary behavioral artifact* of this entire section. Family is, for her, the original compartment.

What follows reconstructs the bonds with the granularity a full-surveillance file would carry, marking inferential confidence where the canon is sparse.

---

### 1. SUSAN MORSE — MOTHER

**Status**: Living (per latest canonical reference, late-period appearance in McCann run; no death panel on record). Estimated late sixties to mid-seventies. Residence inferable as the southeastern United States, most likely a small-city or exurban Georgia address — Subject's incidental speech patterns (the slipped "y'all" under exhaustion in *Hawkeye & Mockingbird* #4; the unconscious softening of vowels when reading aloud to children in the same arc) locate origin in that register, though Subject's adult speech is otherwise SHIELD-flattened mid-Atlantic.

**History and dynamic**: The mother-daughter relationship reads as the structural template for every later intimacy Subject forms — which is to say, a relationship Subject performed competence within rather than was held inside.
