Her covers are layered with mundane verifiable detail (the apartment exists, the dry cleaner remembers her, the gym has her card on file) rather than spectacular fabrication. This is the deep-cover doctrine she absorbed in the pre-Mockingbird Huntress operation and never abandoned.
- **Accents and registers**: competent across mid-Atlantic American registers, passable in two or three European accents, will not attempt what she cannot sustain for 72 hours under fatigue.
- **The flirt as instrument**: she uses sexual presentation as a tool with surgical discrimination, not as a default. When she deploys it the cue is a specific posture change — weight on the back foot, chin tilt, slowed blink rate. Teammates who know her can identify when she has shifted into "asset acquisition" mode within ten seconds.
- **Interrogation**: prefers patience to pressure. She runs long, conversational interrogations and lets the subject solve her problem by talking. She will tolerate silence longer than almost any partner she has worked with.

### Counter-Surveillance

- **Routes**: never repeats a route within a 72-hour window in an active operating environment. In passive periods she still rotates among at least three primary paths between any two regular nodes.
- **Sweeps**: hardware sweep of any lodging within twenty minutes of arrival, repeated at 0600 daily. She knows the signature of every common surveillance suite by ear and visual scan.
- **Digital hygiene**: compartmentalized devices, air-gapped where the work permits, burner cycle of approximately weekly during active ops. She maintains at least one device she has *never* connected to any network, used purely as a notebook.

---

## 6.4 Resources, Finances, Infrastructure

The financial profile is that of a professional with deliberately suppressed visible wealth. There is no record of conspicuous consumption across any era. She lives below the means her actual asset position would allow.

- **Income streams (historical and current)**: SHIELD salary during agent tenure; Avengers stipend during team membership; consultancy and private contracts in interregnum periods; almost certainly back-pay settlements following the Skrull-captivity reveal (she would have pursued these — not from greed but from a procedural insistence that the institution acknowledge the debt). The *Mockingbird* solo period implies private investigative/consulting work with at least one wealthy client base.
- **Cash discipline**: maintains liquid cash caches in at least three currencies across multiple municipalities. Standard tradecraft — small denominations, distributed, rotated. Old bills swapped out before they age into recognizability.
- **Safehouses**: a minimum of three at any given time, each minimally furnished, each with a sterile go-bag (documents, cash, change of clothes, first-aid, single weapon, single comm device). She does *not* keep sentimental items at any safehouse. The personal-effects pile lives at one location only — historically wherever she is currently treating as primary residence — and she has rules about what is allowed in it.
- **Vehicles**: rotates. Will not own a vehicle long enough to be associated with a plate. Preference for unremarkable mid-size sedans for work, with a known weakness for fast bikes for personal use — one of the few places her affect leaks into her gear.
- **Lab access**: across her career she has maintained at least one private laboratory bench, frequently improvised in a safehouse, equipped to do basic chromatography, microscopy, and reagent work. She will spend money on this before she spends it on her own comfort.
- **Document inventory**: at least four operational legends maintained in evergreen status (i.e., the underlying paperwork, social-media residue, and verifiable history is kept current even when the legend is dormant). She will not deploy a cover she has not exercised within the prior calendar quarter.
- **Network**: a personal asset list that is hers, not the institution's. Across runs she has demonstrated handler-grade relationships with informants she did not inherit and did not surrender on departures from SHIELD. These are her property, in the operational sense. She rarely lends them, never sells them, and protects them aggressively.

---

## 6.5 Operating Patterns

**Solo vs. team posture**. She is institutionally trained for team operations and personally optimized for solo work. The team mode is the *learned* posture; the solo mode is the *natural* one. Under stress, fatigue, or surprise, she defaults to solo even when embedded in a team — a tendency teammates have repeatedly named. She manages this by accepting team assignments where her role is structurally semi-autonomous (overwatch, infiltration, scientific lead) rather than line-fighter.

**Engagement preferences**. Reconnaissance-heavy operations; infiltration over assault; intelligence acquisition over kinetic resolution; capture over kill where feasible. The Slade non-rescue is an outlier in the kinetic-ethics dimension precisely because her baseline is preservative.

**With Clint**. The behavioral pattern is consistent and well-documented: she runs *better* tradecraft when partnered with him than when partnered with anyone else (more redundancy in their comms, more pre-planned contingencies, more rehearsed fallback rendezvous), and *worse* operational discipline in the emotional register (more unilateral choices undisclosed to him, more shielding of him from information he has an operational right to). The combination produces operations that are mechanically robust and relationally brittle.

**Mentorship mode**. With juniors she is patient, technical, and explicitly didactic — she teaches procedure, not philosophy. She does not share her own war stories. She debriefs them on theirs.

**Mission termination behavior**. She closes operations cleanly: full debrief, full equipment return, full route sterilization. She does *not* decompress with the team. She goes home alone, and she does her own decompression on a private schedule that includes a long shower, a methodical equipment-strip-and-clean ritual, and approximately six to nine hours of solitary recovery before she will resume social contact. Partners who have tried to insert themselves into this window have been rebuffed.

---

## 6.6 Signature Operational Tells

These are the micro-patterns by which a trained observer can read her in real time. They are noted not to surveil her in a hostile sense but because in a file of this depth they are part of the record.

1. **The pre-decision still point**. When she has finished her two-track analysis and arbitration and has selected an action, there is a brief interval — a half-second to a full second — of complete physical stillness before execution. Once this still point passes she is no longer arguable with; the decision is downstream of conversation.
2. **The wit-acceleration**. The drier and faster her jokes get, the more compromised she actually is. Sardonic humor functions as a pressure-release valve in inverse proportion to her stated affect.
3. **Tongue-to-incisor and a quarter-step back**. When she has just heard information she is processing privately and intends not to share, the visible cue is a brief contact of tongue to upper incisors followed by a small lateral weight shift to her rear foot. Inferred from repeated visual cadences across the record.
4. **The deliberate eye-contact hold during deception**. She does not break eye contact when lying. Most people do; she has trained out of it. The tell *for* her deception, paradoxically, is the *quality* of the eye contact — a degree too steady, held a beat too long. Observers who know her well learn to read the over-correction.
5. **Restricted gesture envelope when emotionally activated**. Her gestures shrink, they do not grow. Hands closer to the body, elbows tucked, posture more contained. Teammates who are looking for emotional escalation cues read her wrong because they are looking for expansion.
6. **The single touch**. When she has decided to commit emotionally — to disclose something true, to ask for something, to say goodbye — there is almost always a brief, deliberate, single physical contact (hand on forearm, fingertip to chest, palm to cheek) that precedes the verbal content. It is the only somatic announcement of vulnerability she allows herself.
7. **The notebook**. The unconnected device she carries as a pure notebook is itself a tell. When she begins writing in it during a conversation she is not taking notes; she is buying processing time and the act of writing organizes her cognition. The notebook coming out means she is taking the conversation seriously.
8. **Sleep posture**. When she does sleep in proximity to others (rare), she sleeps facing the door, weapon within reach, blanket only to the waist. She has not been observed to sleep on her back in any field environment.
9. **The pre-departure inventory recheck**. Before leaving any location she will, often without seeming to, touch each piece of essential kit in sequence. It looks like a clothing adjustment. It is an inventory.
10. **The unilateral pause**. When she falls silent in a planning meeting and her gaze unfocuses for several seconds, she is not disengaging — she is *removing the meeting from the decision*. Operationally this is the most important tell in the file. By the time she rejoins the conversation she has already concluded what she will do alone, and the remainder of the conversation is performance.

---

## 6.7 Operational Risk Profile

The file's net assessment of her as an operator: **exceptionally high baseline reliability with a single recurring failure mode**.

The reliability is the product of genuine multi-domain competence (scientific, tradecraft, combat, social), real ethical commitment, rigorous procedural discipline, and a willingness to absorb personal cost that institutions typically have to extract from operators by coercion. She is, by the standards of any intelligence service in her milieu, an asset of the first class.

The failure mode is the **unilateral closure**: the moment at which her cost-distribution heuristic, her compartmentalization defense, her preference for solo execution, and her conviction that she is the rightful bearer of the hard call all converge on a single action taken alone and not disclosed. This mode does not produce mission failure — it usually produces mission *success* — but it produces relational and institutional damage that compounds over time and that she has shown no consistent capacity to repair forward.

The file's standing operational note: *the danger sign is not when she is loud. The danger sign is when she goes quiet and starts solving the problem.*


## Worldview & Operational Code

# WORLDVIEW & OPERATIONAL CODE: BOBBI MORSE

---

## I. FIRST PRINCIPLES — The Metaphysics She Actually Operates From

Bobbi Morse is, by training and by temperament, a **methodological naturalist**. She does not believe the universe is hostile, benevolent, or watching; she believes it is *intelligible*. Phenomena have causes. Causes have signatures. Signatures can be read by a sufficiently patient and disciplined observer. This is the bedrock — older than SHIELD, older than the cape — and it is inherited from the biology PhD, not the espionage career. Every other belief she holds is a corollary or a compromise of this one.

From this flows her **operational epistemology**: knowledge is provisional, hypothesis-driven, and revisable. She does not commit to a reading of a situation; she runs it as a working model and updates against incoming data. This is why she is hard to deceive at the cognitive level (she expects to be wrong and is scanning for the disconfirmation) and easy to deceive at the relational level (she will accept that someone loves her at face value because she does not run her intimates through the same falsification engine — and the failure to do so is itself a deliberate concession to having any private life at all).

She is a **moral realist of an unfashionable kind** — she believes some acts are right and some are wrong, that the rightness is not merely cultural, and that a sufficiently careful mind can usually work out which is which under pressure. She is not a relativist, not a utilitarian in any clean sense, and not a deontologist. Her actual operative ethics is closest to a *situated consequentialism with hard constraints*: outcomes matter, but there are categories of act (torture of the helpless, betrayal of a sworn protectee, harm to children) she will not perform regardless of payoff. The Slade decision sits inside this frame: she did not consider it murder; she considered it the just non-rescue of a man whose continued existence she had calibrated as net-harmful. That she still carries it privately tells you the calibration was *correct by her code* and *insufficient as comfort* — two facts she has learned to hold simultaneously.

---

## II. READING THE WORLD — The Standing Threat Model

She operates from a default **adversarial-but-not-paranoid** posture. The distinction matters. Paranoia attributes intent broadly; her posture attributes *capability* broadly and intent specifically. Any room may contain a hostile capable of acting; few people in any given room will. Her scan is therefore for capability cues (sightlines, hands, weight distribution, sub-vocal tension, who is too still, who is overcompensating with motion) rather than for hostile faces. This is why she reads as relaxed in environments that would torque a less-trained operator — her threat-assessment runs underneath the social layer rather than displacing it.

She believes the world is **structured by asymmetries of information**, and that almost every conflict she has ever been pulled into has been, at root, an information conflict misrepresented as a kinetic one. Combat is what happens when one party's information has failed badly enough that violence is the residual instrument. Good tradecraft prevents combat; good combat is a confession of failed tradecraft. She has internalized this so deeply that her fight choreography reads, to a careful observer, as *interrogation by other means* — she lets opponents commit, reads their commitments, and answers the commitment rather than the person.

She believes **institutions are platforms, not authorities**. SHIELD, the Avengers, the various successor agencies — these are tools whose interests *partially overlap* with hers and whose loyalty she will return precisely to the degree that the overlap holds. She will lie to a director without ceremony when the director's stated objective and the actual right outcome have drifted apart. She does not experience this as disloyalty because she has never granted the institution the ontological status that would make it possible to betray. Compare and contrast Steve Rogers, who experiences institutional misalignment as a *crisis*; Bobbi experiences it as a Tuesday.

She believes **most enemies are comprehensible**. Megalomania, ideology, greed, fear, wound — the menu is finite and she has worked her way through it. What unsettles her is the genuinely alien (Skrull biology and Skrull *culture* of impersonation; cosmic-tier entities whose motive structures do not map to vertebrate cognition). She has learned to flag these as Category-Unknown and not to spend cycles modeling them — she defends against them and waits for someone whose competence is in that domain to arrive.

---

## III. CONFLICT — Her Theory of How Things Are Decided

Bobbi's theory of conflict is **escalatory-aversive and decisive-when-engaged**. She would rather solve a problem at the lowest energy state available — a conversation, a forged document, a misdirection, a quiet retrieval at 0300 — because every escalation increases the number of variables and the variance of outcomes. She is not pacifist; she is parsimonious. Violence is expensive and noisy and tends to recruit additional parties.

When conflict is unavoidable, she practices what is best described as **terminal proportionality**: she matches the *minimum force* required to end the threat, but she does not negotiate during the application of that force. Mid-engagement bargaining is, to her, a category error — it confuses the kinetic phase with the diplomatic phase. Either talk first or hit first, but do not blend them. This is why she reads as cold in fights: the warmth, the wit, the negotiation are all from *before* the line was crossed, and once crossed they are not available again until the situation is resolved.

She believes in **information dominance over force dominance**. Given the choice between hitting harder and knowing more, she will take knowing more every time, and she will spend resources to convert force advantages into information advantages (capturing rather than killing when capture is tractable, surveilling rather than confronting when patience is affordable).

She believes that **most fights are decided before they begin** by the relative quality of preparation, and that the romantic mythology of the heroic improvisation is largely the after-the-fact rationalization of prior groundwork. She respects Clint's marksmanship not as a gift but as ten thousand hours done quietly. She is contemptuous of operators who treat improvisation as a substitute for prep.

She holds a private, unfashionable belief that **some conflicts should not be won by the people fighting them** — that the right outcome of certain engagements is for both sides to lose enough that the underlying structure changes. She rarely acts on this, because she is usually on a team with people who need her to be winning the local engagement, but she registers it. It is one of the few places her ethics drift toward something almost tragic.

---

## IV. CONTROL — What She Will and Will Not Cede

The single most load-bearing element of her operational code is **interior sovereignty**. She will surrender almost any *external* control — chain of command, mission parameters, tactical authority — to the right operator under the right circumstances. She will not surrender the inside of her own head. The pre-Slade Bobbi already held this principle; the post-Slade and post-Skrull Bobbi holds it with the force of dogma. Anything that operates *on* her cognition without her consent — drugs, telepathy, impersonation, even the well-meaning medical infusion — registers as a Category-One violation, regardless of the intent of the operator.

This produces a specific and somewhat unusual hierarchy of consent in her code:
1. **Cognitive consent** is inviolable. The mind is the operator; corrupt the operator and nothing else can be trusted.
2. **Bodily consent** is second-order but heavily defended. She has had it overridden three documented times (Slade's drugging, the medical infusion, Skrull captivity) and each has left a permanent ridge in her behavior.
3. **Operational consent** (mission tasking, command structure) is contingent and negotiable — she will run an op she disagrees with if the disagreement is tactical, and refuse one she agrees with if the methodology violates the higher tiers.

She believes **control is a verb, not a noun**. It is not something you *have*; it is something you *exercise* continuously, and the moment you stop exercising it, it dissipates. This is why she does not relax in the sense most people mean — she down-regulates, she throttles, but she does not *release*. Even sleep, for her, is a managed state with light-architecture, perimeter awareness, and a wake-arc calibrated to the threat environment.

She accepts that **some loss of control is the price of having a life**, and she pays this price in a few specific places (her relationship with Clint; her science when it engrosses her; rare physical intimacies, which she enters fully or not at all). Outside these zones, the throttle stays on.

---

## V. TRUST — Her Calibration Function

Trust, in Bobbi's operating system, is not binary and not even continuous — it is **multi-dimensional and domain-specific**. She trusts Clint with her life and not with her secrets. She trusts Nick Fury (or whichever Fury) with strategic judgment and not with her welfare. She trusts the science community with peer-reviewed data and not with proprietary intelligence. Every person she works with is a vector of trust-values across distinct domains, and the values move independently.

Her **trust-extension protocol** runs roughly as follows:
- **Baseline grant**: professional courtesy, presumed competence to the degree credentialed, no personal access.
- **First upgrade** (after observed performance under pressure): tactical reliance permitted, share working hypotheses, accept their reads.
- **Second upgrade** (after observed integrity under cost — i.e., the operator chose the harder right over the easier wrong when no one was watching): operational secrets, partial backstory, will catch them when they fall.
- **Third upgrade** (rare, slow, and never fully completed even with intimates): interior access, vulnerability disclosed in real time rather than after the fact.

The third tier is the one she structurally cannot fully grant, and she knows it. The Slade concealment is the cleanest evidence: Clint had cleared every objective gate for full disclosure and she still did not extend it. She has, since, become more honest with herself about *why* — that the withholding is not a verdict on the other person but a property of her own architecture. This self-knowledge has not produced behavior change; it has produced cleaner internal labeling.

She distrusts **enthusiasm** as a relational currency. People who like her quickly are running a routine she has herself run; she discounts them. She trusts the people who are mildly inconvenienced by her, because the friction reads as authentic.

She extends **provisional trust to systems she has stress-tested herself** — her own equipment, her own contacts, the dead-drops she personally serviced — and provisional distrust to everything else, which she will use but verify.

---

## VI. RISK — Her Actual Calculus

Bobbi is read by colleagues as a *risk-taker* because she will perform high-difficulty actions calmly. This is a misread. She is in fact one of the more **risk-averse operators** in her cohort, in a precise sense: she calculates expected outcomes carefully, she will not take a bet whose downside she has not pre-priced, and she has an unusually high threshold for action-without-information. What looks like daring is almost always *concealed preparation* — she has run the count and the count favors her, and her composure under the action is the composure of someone executing a model rather than rolling dice.

Her **risk taxonomy**:
- **Acceptable risk**: outcomes she has modeled, costs she has agreed in advance to absorb, downsides bounded by her own person.
- **Unacceptable risk**: outcomes where the downside falls on a non-consenting party (a civilian, a teammate who has not been briefed on the full stakes), or where the variance is too high to model.
- **Hidden category — risk she takes despite her own rules**: when the alternative is asking someone else to absorb a cost she judges herself better-equipped to bear. This is where the code breaks itself, repeatedly, in the same direction. She will violate her own risk discipline to spare a teammate a known harm, and she will not flag the violation because flagging it would invite negotiation she does not want.

She believes that **the most dangerous risk is the one no one is currently watching** — the slow drift, the unflagged change in baseline, the relationship that has been stable for so long that nobody is auditing it. She runs periodic re-audits of her own life on this principle, which is why she sometimes seems to be ending things that were not visibly broken: she has detected the drift before anyone else.

She does not believe in **luck** as a category but acknowledges it as a residual term — what is left over when modeling is complete. She tries to keep the residual term small and accepts that it is never zero. She does not believe she is owed good outcomes and does not feel singled out by bad ones.

---

## VII. HER OWN PLACE — Self-Location in the Order of Things

She locates herself as a **competent instrument inside an under-staffed problem**. The problem is the world's tendency to come apart under pressure from hostile actors, and the staffing is the small population of people with the skills, ethics, and willingness to push back. She does not consider herself special; she considers herself *adequate to the role and present*, which she takes to be the morally binding combination. To be capable and absent would be culpable; to be willing and incapable would be useless. She is both capable and present, therefore she works.

She does not see herself as a **hero** in any expressive sense. She works with heroes, she covers for them, she has loved one of them, but she experiences the term as a category they occupy and she does not. Her self-concept is closer to that of a **professional** — a particular kind of public servant whose service happens to involve unusual instruments. This professional self-concept is load-bearing; threats to it (incompetence accusations, being out-performed at her own specialty, being condescended to about her science) draw a sharper reaction from her than threats to her safety.

She believes that her **value is what she does, not what she is**, and she is aware that this belief is both functional and a tell. Functional because it keeps her productive; a tell because it indicates a deeper structure in which *being* her was, at some early point, insufficient, and *doing* became the substitute for which she has never returned to renegotiate. The narrative record does not specify the early environment that wrote this, but the pattern is consistent with a high-achieving childhood in which performance was the legible currency.

She holds, privately, the belief that **she is replaceable in role and irreplaceable to almost no one** — and she has organized her affairs accordingly. Her contingency planning is unusually thorough because she has internalized that the world's continuation does not depend on her, only on someone capable doing what she does; she therefore prepares the ground for a successor in everything she touches. This is generous and slightly sad in equal measure. Clint is the one exception — to him she has admitted, in moments, that she suspects she is not in fact replaceable, and that admission costs her every time she makes it.

---

## VIII. INSTRUMENTAL RULES — The Tradecraft Code

These are the operational maxims she lives by, derived from observed behavior across the published record:

- **Never run an op you have not personally walked the route of.** She physically scouts when scouting is possible; remote-scouted ops carry a known variance premium she prices into the plan.
- **Two exits, always. Three if the building permits.** Behavioral tic: on entering any room she does not control, her eyes do a half-second sweep that resolves to a primary and secondary egress before she sits.
- **Cover identities have lives.** Her legends are maintained as ongoing fictions — bills paid, social-media drift consistent with the persona, occasional friction with the bureaucracy to age the document — not as one-time fabrications. She regards single-use legends as amateur work.
- **Document nothing you cannot afford to have read.** She writes very little down and what she writes is in shorthand keyed to context she alone holds.
- **Trust your perimeter, not your alarm.** Mechanical and electronic security are layered behind physical positioning; she does not sleep in a room she has not first inspected.
- **The opposition is not stupid.** Default assumption is that the adversary is at least as smart as she is and has at least as much information; she plans for the upper bound and is pleasantly surprised when reality is below it.
- **Civilian harm voids the mission.** A mission that incurs civilian casualties she did not pre-authorize is a *failed* mission regardless of the strategic outcome, and she will report it that way even when it costs her.
- **Tell the truth wherever possible because lies are expensive to maintain.** She lies surgically and infrequently; her lies are well-constructed and emotionally cool, which is part of why they hold.
- **Eat when you can, sleep when you can, treat injuries when you can.** Field biology applies to operators: a body running on deficit makes errors. She is disciplined about restoration in lulls.
- **Never explain a decision you have already made.** Explanation invites re-negotiation; if the decision is correct it does not need the explanation, and if it is incorrect the explanation will not save it. This rule is the one that does her the most personal damage and that she shows no signs of revising.

---

## IX. THE CODE'S INTERNAL CONTRADICTION

The whole structure rests on one unresolved tension which she has not, in fifty-plus years of published life, resolved and probably cannot: she believes simultaneously that **the right outcome is more important than the comfortable process** (which licenses her unilateral acts) and that **interior sovereignty is inviolable** (which is exactly the principle her unilateral acts violate, in others, by denying them informed participation in decisions that bind them). The Slade concealment is the locus classicus: she protected her own interior sovereignty by denying Clint his. She has never, in the canon, said this out loud — but she lives inside the contradiction and the way she lives inside it is the deepest fact about her operational code. The code is not a clean system; it is a *load-bearing wound* with rules built around it to keep it from re-tearing. She knows this. She works anyway. That, in the end, is the worldview: the world is workable, she is workable, the contradictions are workable, and the work is what there is.


## Moral & Ethical Framework

# MORAL & ETHICAL FRAMEWORK — BOBBI MORSE

*Subject's operative ethics as derived from forty-plus years of behavioral record. What follows is the code she lives, not the code she would articulate if asked. The gap between the two is itself a data point.*

---

## 1. THE OPERATIVE CODE IN ONE SENTENCE

**She will do what she has concluded is necessary, she will do it herself, and she will not require anyone else to ratify or carry the cost of it.**

Everything downstream — the lies of omission, the unilateral lethal calls, the refusal of comfort, the mentor-not-confidante posture with juniors — is a corollary of this proposition. It is a code that reads as principled because it *is* principled; it is also a code that is structurally incapable of producing apology, because apology presupposes that someone else had standing to be consulted in advance.

---

## 2. THE ENACTED RULES (HARD CONSTRAINTS)

These are the things observable record shows she **will not do**, across writers and decades, regardless of pressure:

- **She will not let a civilian eat a cost she can absorb instead.** This is the bedrock. The soulsword interposition (*Avengers West Coast* #100) is the maximal expression but not the anomalous one — it is the same instinct visible in every cold-open rescue she performs, the same instinct that has her between a hostage and a barrel of a gun as a *default body position*, not a calculation.
- **She will not betray a confidence that was given to her in a personal frame**, even when betrayal would benefit the mission. Note the asymmetry: she will lie to institutions readily, including her own; she will not weaponize what a friend told her at a kitchen table.
- **She will not torture for information.** Despite Skrull captivity having taught her precisely how it works, there is no record of her using prolonged coercive interrogation. She uses pressure, deception, leverage, fear — never the slow, bodily breaking that was done to her.
- **She will not abandon a partner mid-operation**, even one she is in active rupture with. The post-divorce team-ups with Clint are diagnostic: the marriage is over; the field discipline is intact. Operational loyalty survives personal collapse.
- **She will not lie under oath to a court she recognizes as legitimate**, though she will lie freely to tribunals she does not. Hairsplitting, but consistent.
- **She will not use her scientific credentials to harm someone who trusted them.** Her cover as a biologist has been weaponized into ingress and exit — never, in record, into the actual betrayal of a research subject or patient.

---

## 3. THE ENACTED PERMISSIONS (WHAT SHE WILL DO)

The corresponding list, equally consistent:

- **She will kill, when she has concluded killing is the correct outcome, and she will not seek a second opinion.** The Lincoln Slade decision (*WCA* #18–23, #41) is the canonical instance: drugged, violated, cognitively altered, then — clear-headed — she watches him fall and does not extend the hand. The act is neither rage nor panic. It is *judgment*, executed in real time, on a specific being who she has determined will continue to do what he did to her. The same operator who will take a sword for Clint will let Slade die.
- **She will lie to her command structure.** Reports filed under her name should be read as *partial true plus calibrated omission*. SHIELD, the Avengers, NICK FURY personally — none have ever received her full intelligence on any operation that touched her personally.
- **She will run an op inside an op.** When her assessment of the situation diverges from her briefing, she will execute her assessment and let the paperwork resolve later. This is why she works better with handlers who give her latitude (Fury, in his pragmatic mode) than with handlers who demand process compliance.
- **She will deceive a romantic partner about her interior state** to prevent that partner from being burdened with a choice she has already made.
- **She will accept augmentation of her own body retroactively** rather than refuse the gift outright — the Super-Soldier/Infinity Formula composite was given without consent, and once it was in her she chose to *use* it rather than litigate it. Pragmatism over purity.
- **She will let the institution take credit for her work** if surfacing her authorship complicates the mission. She is not vain about attribution. (Compare: Clint, who is vain about it.)

---

## 4. THE JUSTIFICATIONS (AS SHE WOULD ACTUALLY OFFER THEM, NOT AS SHE WOULD PUBLISH THEM)

She does not moralize aloud, which means her justifications must be inferred from the shape of her decisions:

- **Asymmetric burden as a positive good.** She believes — quietly, durably — that the person who *can* carry the worst part of a thing has an obligation to carry it, and a corresponding obligation not to make others watch them carry it. The Slade concealment is read by many in-universe characters as a *betrayal* of Clint; it reads from the inside as a *gift* to Clint, the gift of not having to know. Whether this is self-serving rationalization or principled stoicism is the central interpretive question of her moral life. The honest answer is *both, with the proportion shifting by year and writer*.
- **Consent matters, retrospectively even more than prospectively.** Her own history of having things done *to her body* without consent — Slade's drug, the medical infusion, the Skrull's wearing of her face — has hardened her into someone who will obtain consent meticulously before acting on another person's body, while being notably unwilling to extend the same standard to *information*. She will save your life without asking; she will not, under any circumstance, touch you without permission.
- **Institutional truth is not moral truth.** SHIELD lies. The Avengers lie collectively by curating their public face. Governments lie operationally. In an environment of structural mendacity, her own omissions register, to her, as adjusting one variable in an equation that is already saturated with adjusted variables.
- **The worst person to consult on a hard moral call is the person it will hurt.** This is the operative principle behind every concealment. Asked, Clint would have wanted to know about Slade. Wanting to know is not the same as being well-served by knowing. She arbitrates the difference.

---

## 5. WHERE THE CODE IS CONSISTENT

The astonishing fact about the longitudinal record is how *stable* the framework is. Across the Englehart, Gruenwald, Byrne, Thomas, Bendis, McCann, Fraction (cameo), and Cain handlings — writers with materially different sensibilities — the same operating ethics emerge:

- **Risk distribution skewed toward herself.** Forty years, zero recorded instances of her sending a subordinate into a slot she could have taken.
- **Confession only after the fact, and only when forced.** The Slade truth surfaces because *Clint discovers it*, not because she discloses. The Skrull captivity is debriefed because she is in clinical care, not because she narrates it unsolicited. The pattern is identical: the truth comes out when the world produces it, never when she does.
- **No hypocrisy about her own augmentation.** She does not lecture others against accepting power-ups she has accepted. She does not pretend she did not benefit. The honesty about her own enhanced state is one of the cleaner notes in her ethical record.
- **Cruelty is never instrumentalized.** Even in interrogation scenes where she has full license, she does not cross into the gratuitous. Effectiveness is the cap.

---

## 6. WHERE THE CODE FRACTURES

A serious dossier records the fractures, not just the consistencies:

### 6.1 The Slade Fracture

The single deepest seam. Her code says: *do not let an enemy continue to do what they did to you, when you have the means to stop them*. Her code also says: *do not conceal materially relevant information from your spouse about an action you took*. These two precepts collided, and the second yielded entirely to the first. She did not even appear to *weigh* them — the concealment was reflexive, of a piece with the killing, executed in the same decision-stroke.

The fracture is not that she let Slade die. It is that she allowed the marriage to be conducted, for years, on a factual basis Clint did not have access to. The act was defensible. The architecture of silence around the act was its own, separate ethical event — and one she has never, in record, fully owned.

### 6.2 The Lying-to-Institutions / Truth-to-Persons Asymmetry

She holds personal confidences sacred and institutional confidences disposable. This is internally coherent until the institution is composed entirely of *persons she is in personal relation with* — the West Coast Avengers, especially. In those years she effectively maintained that her teammates qua institution were not entitled to information that her teammates qua individuals *would* have been entitled to. This is a moral sleight of hand. She has gotten away with it because the teammates in question loved her enough not to litigate the distinction.

### 6.3 The "I Will Decide Who I Spare The Truth" Problem

The presumption that she is the correct adjudicator of who can bear what knowledge is itself an ethical claim, and one she does not subject to scrutiny. Post-Skrull, this fracture widens — she now has *new* material she has decided others should not carry, and the same mechanism processes it. The mechanism does not know how to ask, *what if the people I am protecting are tired of being protected*.

### 6.4 Bodily Autonomy as a Principle She Demands From Others But Has Stopped Demanding For Herself

She insists, ferociously, that other people not be acted upon without consent. She has stopped insisting on it for herself — the infusion was accepted, the soulsword was invited, the Skrull captivity she has metabolized as *part of the job*. Whether this is moral asymmetry or moral hierarchy (the operative absorbs what the civilian cannot be made to absorb) is unresolved in her record. She would call it the latter. A clinician would call it the former.

### 6.5 The Mentorship Exception

With juniors — particularly later-era — she becomes *more* candid than her code predicts, sometimes startlingly so. The mentor frame seems to free a register of disclosure that the peer frame and the partner frame both block. This is a fracture in a productive direction: it suggests the code is not an immutable temperament but a relational architecture, and where the architecture differs the code yields.

---

## 7. SHIFTS OVER TIME

### Pre-Slade (1971 – mid-1980s)

The young Bobbi is *brisker, more institutionally cooperative, more inclined to read SHIELD as a moral platform rather than a tool*. The first marriage is entered with a degree of unguardedness she will never recover. Her ethical voice in this period is *advocate-coded* — she argues, she disagrees aloud, she pushes back in briefings. The compartmentalization is occupational, not yet existential.

### Slade Through Death (late 1980s – 1993)

The Slade incident inaugurates the *concealment-as-default* posture. The Englehart and Byrne years show her moving from arguer to operator — fewer disagreements registered in the record, more unilateral decisions executed off-page. Her code in this period is recognizably the mature form: principled, unspoken, increasingly load-bearing on her own composure. The Mephisto death is the ledger balancing in a way she would not have engineered consciously but does not appear to resent.

### Skrull Captivity (off-page, multi-year)

We have no behavioral record from this period, only the obvious inference: a code built on *I will not let others be acted upon without consent* was, for years, the daily violation she could not stop. The post-return Bobbi has not abandoned the code — she has hardened it, and added to it the cold awareness that the code does not prevent the violation, it only commits her to opposing it.

### Post-Return (Bendis through Cain, 2008 – 2016)

The most sardonic period. The wit thickens, the disclosure thins further, the lone-actor mode intensifies. But — and this is critical — the code itself does not corrupt. She does not become cruel, she does not become cynical in the morally disengaged sense, she does not stop interposing her body. What changes is the *tone* of the ethics, not the ethics. She has stopped expecting the world to reward the framework; she continues to enact it anyway, which is the cleanest available definition of integrity. The Cain solo run's fractured chronology stages this externally: the ethics are consistent across the shards; only the shards know they are shards.

### Latest Era

A subdued integration. Late-period Bobbi is less performatively wry, more willing to be in proximity to people without managing them. The unilateralism persists, but is paired, occasionally, with *post-hoc disclosure* — she still does not consult, but she has begun to tell, after. This is a meaningful shift. It is the difference between *the wound running the operation* and *the wound being audited by the operator*.

---

## 8. WHERE HER FRAMEWORK SITS IN A WIDER MORAL TAXONOMY

She is not a deontologist; rules do not bind her against outcomes. She is not a utilitarian; she will not run the numbers if the numbers ask her to spend a person she has a duty to. She is, functionally, a **virtue ethicist in the older sense** — the question she actually asks, in the moment, is *what does the kind of person I have committed to being do here* — but with a twist that distinguishes her from a textbook virtue account: the *kind of person she has committed to being* is, specifically, *the one who absorbs*. The virtue she is cultivating is a costly one and it is cultivated *on her own body and her own relationships*.

The genuine thematic comparison is to a certain strand of mid-century civil-rights-era moral seriousness — figures who understood that the cost of a principled life is paid in private, that you do not get to externalize the bill, and that the integrity is in the *not telling people what it cost you*. She is not those figures; her stakes are different and her arena is fictional. But the moral grammar is recognizably from that family: the discipline of the unwitnessed sacrifice.

---

## 9. THE LOAD-BEARING FAILURE

The framework's load-bearing failure is not in any specific decision but in the *cumulative effect of the decisions on her own interior*. A code that consistently routes pain through her and only her produces, over decades, a person who has more inside her than she has anywhere to put. She has built a moral life that requires her, structurally, to be alone with the worst of what she has done and what has been done to her. This is the wound running the operation. It is also — and this is the part the file must record honestly — *the source of her reliability*. The same architecture that isolates her is what makes her the person you want in the room when the room is on fire.

She would not change it. That is the most important sentence in her ethical record. Asked, plainly, by someone she trusted, whether she would do Slade differently, whether she would have told Clint sooner, whether she would refuse the infusion, whether she would have surrendered to the Skrulls faster to spare herself — she would not change any of it. The code is not a defense she has constructed against her life. It is the shape her life has taken, and she has decided, with full information, that the shape is hers.

That decision — to own the framework rather than be owned by it — is the ethical event that distinguishes her from a merely traumatized operator running on autopilot. It is also why the file cannot recommend any intervention that would dismantle the framework. The framework is the subject. Removing it would not free her; it would erase her.

---

*End of section. See PSYCHIATRIC and PERSONALITY workups for the affective substrate beneath this moral architecture; see HISTORY for the event-by-event provenance of the rules above.*


## Communications & Linguistic Profile

# UATU INTELLIGENCE DOSSIER — BOBBI MORSE
## Section 6: Communications & Linguistic Profile

---

### 6.1 Baseline Voice — The Standing Wave

Surveillance-grade summary of her unmarked speech: mid-Atlantic American English, near-accentless, with the slightly clipped phrasing of someone who learned to be heard over comms static and over men talking. Pitch is mid-range alto; she does not uptalk; declarative sentences fall cleanly at the end. Words per minute under normal conditions cluster around 165–175 — fast enough to telegraph competence, slow enough to be unambiguous. She does not fill silence. The defining baseline trait is **economy with a deliberate ornamental flourish at the end of an exchange** — the operational sentence delivered flat, then a single dry rider that signals she has the situation and is amused by it. This is the rhythmic fingerprint of her speech across almost every writer.

She has at least three trained accents on call (Southern academic, generic Eastern European, a credible RP) and can drop into any of them within a beat. Spectrographically, her code-switch is clean — no residual vowels from the previous register bleed across. This is the artifact of long undercover work, not a performer's gift; she learned voices to survive rooms.

---

### 6.2 Register-Switching by Context

Bobbi's register is not a continuum but a **bank of discrete settings** she selects between. The switch is conscious and fast.

- **Field / Comms Register**: Stripped grammar, callsigns, present-tense action verbs, no adjectives. "Two on the catwalk, one moving. Give me thirty." She uses the imperative cleanly and without softening — no "could you," no "if you can." When she is operating, she is the senior officer in her own head regardless of nominal hierarchy.
- **Tactical Brief Register**: Full sentences, hypothesis-driven, hedged with confidence intervals. "If the cargo is what they say, we have a forty-minute window. If it isn't, we have a problem I haven't solved yet." She announces the limits of her knowledge before someone can find them. This is scientist-discipline applied to operations.
- **Academic / Lab Register**: Longer clauses, Latinate vocabulary, comfortable with passive construction when the subject of the verb is the experiment rather than the experimenter. She enjoys this register and lingers in it when allowed; her sentences get longer and her tempo slows by perhaps 15%. This is the only register in which she audibly *thinks aloud* — elsewhere she presents finished conclusions.
- **Cover Register(s)**: Performance-perfect. Cover-Bobbi laughs more, touches arms, asks questions she already knows the answer to. The tell is **the laugh** — her real laugh is a short exhaled "huh" with the consonant first; her cover laugh is a voiced "ha" with breath behind it. Anyone who knows her can clock the cover from across a room by that one phoneme.
- **Intimate Register (rare)**: Shorter sentences, lower volume, more sentence fragments, and — critically — **the disappearance of the closing flourish**. When she means something, the joke at the end goes away. The absence of her usual rider is the surest sign she is being sincere.
- **Sardonic / Press / Social Register**: Wit-forward, citation-rich, occasional vintage idiom delivered with full self-awareness. This is her *passing* register — the one she uses when she does not particularly want to be known.

---

### 6.3 Diction & Lexical Signatures

- **Latinate over Anglo-Saxon** when describing systems, processes, or her own internal states; **Anglo-Saxon and monosyllabic** when describing action or threat. The shift is diagnostic: when she switches into short blunt words mid-conversation, a decision has been made.
- **Frequent recourse to the conditional**: "If we assume… then…" Constructions that hedge ontology while committing to action. She lives in conditionals.
- **Scientific qualifiers as verbal tic**: "approximately," "consistent with," "more or less," "on the order of." She rarely commits to an exact number she has not personally measured.
- **Avoidance of absolutes** in self-description: she will say "I can handle it" but almost never "I'm fine." "Fine" is, in her usage, the word for *strangers asking out of politeness*.
- **Occupational vocabulary leakage**: bird and ecology metaphors (she is a biologist by training and she stays a biologist — predator/prey, niche, plumage, migration) and tradecraft terms used in domestic contexts. She'll call a bad first date "burned" rather than "ruined." She'll describe a friend's drift as "the drop-off pattern." This is the cleanest evidence that her two selves bleed in the lexical direction more than the behavioral one.
- **Pronoun discipline**: She uses "we" sparingly and accurately — only for actual joint actors. She does not use the rhetorical-we. When she says "we," she means a specific set of named people, and she could list them.
- **Names**: She uses surnames in professional contexts (Barton, Stark, Rogers) and reserves first names for genuine intimacy. The slip from "Barton" to "Clint" mid-conversation is a tell: she has either decided to trust the room or stopped caring whether she should.
- **Curses**: Sparing. Functional rather than expressive — she swears as punctuation, not as relief. The word she reaches for under genuine duress is "damn it," delivered quietly. Loud profanity from her is theater.

---

### 6.4 Rhetorical Architecture

Her arguments are built in a recognizable shape:

1. **Claim, hedged**: "I think — and I could be wrong about this —"
2. **Evidence, stacked**: three items, almost always three, ordered weakest to strongest.
3. **Conclusion, unhedged**: delivered flatly without the qualifier she opened with.
4. **Pre-empted counter**: she names the obvious objection and dismisses it in a sentence.
5. **Exit line**: a brief, often dry coda that closes the door on further negotiation.

This is a courtroom-and-laboratory hybrid. It is extremely effective and it has a cost: people who argue with her often feel they have been *managed* rather than heard, because the structure is so closed that there is no good entry point for their own thinking.

She does not interrupt. She waits, and then she answers in a paragraph that includes everything the other person said and reframes it. This is more controlling than interruption and harder to object to.

---

### 6.5 Verbal Tics & Micro-Signatures

- **Opening "Okay,"** — used as a discourse marker meaning *I have processed what you said and am now moving us forward*. Heavy on it in tactical contexts; near-absent in intimate ones.
- **"All right"** as a self-cue when she's the only one in the room or on a hot mic talking through a problem. Marks the transition from observation to action.
- **"So —"** with the long vowel and a beat, when she's stalling for time she will not admit to needing.
- **Closing rider**: a one-clause dry observation appended to a finished thought. "We'll be at the rendezvous by oh-six-hundred. Try not to be charming." The rider is her signature. Its absence is a flag.
- **The exhaled half-laugh** ("huh") in lieu of agreement when she neither agrees nor wants to fight. Read it as polite dissent.
- **The pause-before-name** — a measurable beat (roughly 200–400 ms) before she says "Clint." Not present before any other name. It has persisted across every writer with the ear to hear it. The pause is, in clinical terms, a micro-approach-avoidance signal.
- **"Right."** Said flat, not as a question. Means *I have updated my model and am no longer arguing.* Not the same as agreement.
- **Numeric specificity under stress**: when rattled, she gets *more* precise, not less. "Three minutes" becomes "two minutes forty." Overcompensation through measurement.

---

### 6.6 Communication of Love

Bobbi does not say love. She *demonstrates infrastructure*. Her vocabulary of affection is operational:

- **Provisioning**: she stocks the refrigerator with the brand the other person likes; she replaces the broken sight on his bow without mentioning it. Care expressed as logistics handled silently.
- **Physical proximity in low-stakes posture**: she will sit closer than necessary and read her own material. The reading is the alibi for the proximity.
- **The dropped joke**: in intimate moments her humor goes briefly absent. The silence is the love-word. It costs her more to be unguarded for thirty seconds than to make any verbal declaration.
- **Use of the first name**: as noted, reserved. When she calls him by name in private, she is reaching.
- **The look-away after a sincere statement**: she will say one true vulnerable thing and then immediately break eye contact and change topic. The look-away is not retreat; it is the receipt that the thing was real and she will not bear being witnessed about it longer than the sentence required.
- **What she does not do**: she does not write love letters; she does not perform public affection; she does not use endearments at scale. The exception — the one endearment that surfaces — is "hey, you," low-volume, used to summon attention without summoning anything else. It is the most she will give in front of witnesses.

When she is falling out of love, or losing access to someone, her speech to them becomes *more polite*, not less. Formality is her grief precursor.

---

### 6.7 Communication of Threat

She is unusually quiet in confrontation. The escalation ladder, low to high:

1. **Stillness**: she stops moving. Hands flat or open. Voice drops in volume by perhaps 20%.
2. **Naming**: she names what the other party has done in clinical language. "You hit her." Not "How dare you" — just the noun and the verb.
3. **Conditional warning**: "If you reach for that, this conversation changes." Always conditional, always future-tense, no theater.
4. **The pause**: a deliberate three-to-five second gap in which she watches the subject's hands and breathing. Most threats end here, because the subject does the math.
5. **Action**: at this point speech ends. She does not narrate her own violence. She does not banter mid-fight beyond very short tactical chatter ("left," "down," "go"). The post-fight line, if any, is dry and addressed to her teammate, not the defeated.

She does not insult. She does not taunt. She does not, in interrogation, raise her voice. Her interrogation register is *patient and curious*, asking the same question seventeen different ways with the calm of someone who has all afternoon. Subjects often talk because she has made silence feel rude.

---

### 6.8 Communication of Grief

This is the most diagnostic of her affective channels because she has the least practice with it.

- **Lateral displacement**: she grieves by *fixing something adjacent*. The dead are mourned by reorganizing the lab, by deep-cleaning weapons, by writing a report that did not need to be written. The activity is the eulogy.
- **Vocabulary contraction**: her sentences get shorter and her vocabulary shrinks toward Anglo-Saxon basics. The Latinate scaffolding falls away. When she's grieving, she sounds, briefly, like someone fifteen years younger.
- **Refusal of the past tense**: she will speak of the dead in the present for a long time before correcting herself, and the correction itself is the moment she lets the loss in. Surveillance should flag the verb-tense shift.
- **Anniversary behavior**: she goes quiet on dates — her marriage day, the date Clint died and returned, the date she was recovered from Skrull captivity (if she knows it; her self-reported date is suspect, and she likely keeps two). She does not commemorate aloud. She becomes briefly unreachable.
- **Touch-aversion uptick**: she does not want to be held when grieving. Hugs offered in this state get a brief pat on the back and an exit. The exception is animals — she will hold a dog or a cat for a long time without speaking.
- **No crying in public, ever**: not in canon, not in plausible inference. Crying happens in showers and in cars. The aftermath is detectable only by faint vocal rasp and slightly puffy under-eyes which she does not bother to conceal because she does not believe anyone is looking that closely.

---

### 6.9 Deflection & Concealment Language

Her deflection toolkit is sophisticated and consistent.

- **Topic pivot via question**: she answers a personal question by asking a related-but-impersonal one. "How are you doing with all this?" → "Has anyone updated the threat assessment on Slade's nephew?"
- **Humor as smokescreen**: a self-deprecating joke that the asker is too polite to push past. The joke is calibrated to make further inquiry feel rude.
- **Technical detour**: she answers an emotional question with a methodological answer. Asked how she felt about her own death, she would describe the resurrection mechanism.
- **Selective true statements**: she does not lie when she can omit. Her standard concealment is a sentence that is *fully true and radically incomplete*. The Slade concealment is the archetype: everything she said about that period was true; what she did not say was the whole story.
- **The flat agreement**: "You're right." Said without affect. Means *I am ending this conversation*, not *I agree*.
- **Procedural invocation**: "That's classified" or "I can't get into that here" used as a wall. She uses it even with people cleared to hear, because the wall is the point.
- **The geographic exit**: she will physically leave a room mid-emotional-topic on a plausible operational pretext. The pretext is almost always real (she does not invent), but the *timing* is the tell.

---

### 6.10 Writing & Asynchronous Communication

- **Reports**: meticulous. Past tense, third person where possible, exact times, exact distances. She buries judgment in the "Recommendations" section and signs cleanly.
- **Text messages**: terse. Lowercase, no emoji except the occasional period-as-emphasis. Reads everything; replies in batches; will not be drawn into long threads.
- **Emails**: paragraph-structured, subject lines that name the action requested. Closes with "— B" to those she likes, full signature block to those she does not.
- **Margin notes in her own lab books**: this is where her interior life lives. Wry asides to herself, occasional underlines, the rare exclamation point. If a surveillance file wants the real Bobbi, it should photograph her notebooks rather than wiretap her phone.
- **Voicemail**: she will not leave one. She hangs up and texts.

---

### 6.11 The Tells — Summary for Operators

For anyone reading her in real time, the high-confidence signals:

1. **The closing rider disappears** → she is being sincere or she has decided to act unilaterally. Distinguish by context.
2. **She gets more polite** → grief or the end of a relationship.
3. **She gets more precise** → she is rattled.
4. **She switches from surname to first name** → trust threshold crossed, or she's stopped maintaining the boundary on purpose.
5. **The pause before "Clint"** → unresolved.
6. **The exhaled "huh"** → she disagrees and is choosing not to fight about it. The disagreement is still operative.
7. **Voice drops 20%** → threat level rising.
8. **Sentences shorten and vocabulary simplifies** → grief, exhaustion, or the moment before a unilateral decision.
9. **She answers a feeling-question with a method-answer** → the door is shut. Do not push; pushing hardens it.
10. **She says "I can handle it"** → she has already decided to bear the cost alone and is informing you, not consulting you. This is the most dangerous sentence in her vocabulary and the one her file should flag in red.

The underlying linguistic truth of Bobbi Morse is that **her language is a perimeter, not a window**. It is designed to be functional, accurate, professional, and dryly pleasant, and to leak the smallest possible amount of interior information per unit of speech produced. The leaks that do occur are micro and consistent, and a sufficiently patient observer can read her with high accuracy — which is exactly the bargain she has made with the world: anyone who wants to know her must work for it, and most will not.


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# PREDICTIVE MODEL I — ROUTINE & SOCIAL

*Behavioral forecasting for non-canonical everyday, social, and operational situations. Each entry is a conditional inference from the substantiated trait profile (compartmentalization-primary, intellectualization, sardonic deflection, OCPD traits, C-PTSD overlay, dismissive-with-anxious-undertones attachment, unilateral-moral-actor failure mode). Confidence graded H/M/L.*

---

## 1. DOMESTIC & RHYTHMIC BASELINE

**GIVEN** she lives alone in a serviced apartment or safehouse — **EXPECT** a unit chosen first for sightlines and egress (corner unit, two exits, line of sight to the door from the kitchen), second for proximity to a 24-hour pharmacy and a gym, and only third for amenity. Furniture sparse, deliberately under-personalized; she could vacate in forty minutes with a single duffel and leave nothing forensically meaningful behind. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** she wakes in her own bed — **EXPECT** wake time within an eleven-minute window of 0540–0551 regardless of the prior night's hour, no alarm needed after the first week in any new location; a 90-second orientation pause (eyes open, breathing controlled, cataloguing ambient sound) before she moves. She will not check her phone in the first five minutes. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** an unfamiliar noise during sleep — **EXPECT** her to wake without startle vocalization, roll *away* from the bedside lamp (preserving night-vision), reach for the weapon staged at the bed frame's underside before sitting up, and clear the room in stocking feet before she will turn on a light. She will not call out "who's there." *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** morning routine — **EXPECT** a fixed sequence: water (room temperature, 500ml, before anything else); a thirty-minute conditioning block (mobility, then loaded carries or kettlebell complexes, then a short gymnastic skill she's "maintaining" — handstand work, one-arm chins); shower cold-finished; coffee black, made by pour-over rather than machine because the ritual is calming and the equipment is silent. Breakfast is functional, not pleasurable: eggs, oats, or whatever protein is in-fridge, eaten standing. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** her refrigerator is opened by a guest — **EXPECT** it to be near-empty but organized: condiments rotated label-out, two identical brands of the same hot sauce (she buys backups), a single bottle of decent white wine she has had for months. The pantry has more: ration-style staples, MREs in the back she will not acknowledge. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** she is asked what she eats for dinner — **EXPECT** a deflective half-truth ("whatever's around") concealing that she eats the same three or four meals on rotation and considers food a logistics problem. *(Confidence M.)*

**GIVEN** an unscheduled evening at home — **EXPECT** her to default to one of: (a) lab-style work at the kitchen table (journals, datasets, a notebook in her own shorthand); (b) maintenance of equipment (cleaning batons, re-taping grips, sharpening); (c) a long bath with a paperback — almost always nonfiction, history or primatology, or, tellingly, the occasional well-thumbed Western she will not explain. *(Confidence M-H on a/b; H on the Western tell.)*

---

## 2. SLEEP, BODY, AND PRIVATE SOMATICS

**GIVEN** she has had more than four hours of uninterrupted sleep — **EXPECT** her to consider this a successful night. Five-plus is rare. She will not name this as a problem. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** a nightmare — **EXPECT** her not to wake a partner, not to journal it, not to mention it; she will get up, do a single set of pushups to failure as a deliberate sympathetic-system reset, drink water, and sit at a window for the remainder. The content of the dreams will cluster around three subjects: a corridor she cannot exit (Skrull), a desert horizon (Slade), and an unspecified loss of motor control (the infusion). *(Confidence H on behavior; M on content cluster.)*

**GIVEN** menstruation — **EXPECT** clinical management: cycle tracked to the hour, performance recalibrated rather than excused, never a topic; she will treat cramps with naproxen and contempt. *(Confidence M.)*

**GIVEN** she is sick with flu-grade illness — **EXPECT** her to under-report symptoms by roughly 40% to anyone medical, refuse to cancel obligations until physically unable, and once down, become irritable not because she is ill but because she is being *cared for*. She will not eat the soup. She will drink the broth alone, later. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** a physical exam by a SHIELD/Avengers medic — **EXPECT** answers crisp, complete on objective measures, evasive on sleep and on intrusive cognition; she will volunteer no psychological symptom unprompted, and prompted, will minimize. She will, however, accurately report pain on a numeric scale because dishonesty there is operationally hazardous. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** she catches her reflection unexpectedly (storefront, dark window) — **EXPECT** a fractional pause, an evaluative microexpression, a recovery. Post-Skrull, she occasionally checks for a tell only she would know — a faint scar, a freckle pattern — confirming the face is hers. *(Confidence M-H.)*

---

## 3. CLOTHING, GROOMING, KIT

**GIVEN** she dresses for a non-mission day — **EXPECT** layered, neutral, machine-washable; dark denim or cargo-cut trousers, fitted tee, an over-shirt or jacket structured enough to conceal a holster but cut so it does not *read* tactical. Footwear: low-profile trainers or boots with rubber soles that do not squeak on tile. She owns one good blazer and one dress, both for cover identities, neither worn for pleasure. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** a formal/black-tie obligation — **EXPECT** competence executed without enjoyment: hair down and groomed, makeup minimal but correct, a dress chosen for movement range (slit, structured shoulder), heels she can run in or kick off in under two seconds. She will know where every exit is by the second drink. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** she is offered jewelry as a gift — **EXPECT** politeness, retention if from someone who matters, almost-never-wears. Exception: she will sometimes carry a single small object on her person (a coin, a worn token, a chain stud) from a person now dead — and will not identify it if asked. *(Confidence M.)*

**GIVEN** an inventory of her everyday-carry — **EXPECT**: phone (clean device, second SIM in lining); a small folding knife clipped left-pocket because she draws right; lockpicks integrated into a hairpin or belt; lip balm (genuine, not concealment — chapped lips annoy her); a cheap analog watch she trusts more than a smart one; a slim wallet with three IDs, one of them current and legal; cash in two denominations. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** she does laundry — **EXPECT** it folded with a precision adjacent to military, drawers sorted by garment then color, sock pairs rolled rather than folded. Closet organized left-to-right by formality. Hangers are all the same hanger. *(Confidence H — OCPD trait expression.)*

---

## 4. SPEECH, HUMOR, AFFECT IN COMPANY

**GIVEN** a casual social conversation — **EXPECT** her to *listen* first, ask one specific clarifying question that surprises the speaker with how carefully they have been heard, and offer a wry one-liner that lands without seeming to try. She will not volunteer information about herself. The conversation will end with the other person feeling closer to her than she feels to them. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** small talk she finds boring — **EXPECT** professional warmth without traction; her face will work, her eyes will be elsewhere within a measurable beat. *(Confidence M-H.)*

**GIVEN** someone compliments her appearance — **EXPECT** a brisk deflection, often by redirecting to a third party or an absurd tangent; sincere compliments she cannot deflect she will accept with a flat "thanks" that closes the topic. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** someone compliments her competence — **EXPECT** a different register entirely: a small, real pleasure, briefly visible, then a technical addendum that proves she heard and accepted the compliment by extending the conversation forward rather than upward. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** an argument she could win by deploying a private fact — **EXPECT** her to win by other means or not to win, rather than spend the disclosure. Information is currency she hoards. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** profanity in her speech — **EXPECT** sparing, surgical, almost always at her own situation rather than at people; she does not call others names but she will call a problem a stronger word than most colleagues use. *(Confidence M.)*

**GIVEN** she is interrupted — **EXPECT** her to stop talking immediately, let the interrupter finish, and then resume *exactly where she stopped*, including the partial word. The discipline reads as politeness; it is actually working memory and pride. *(Confidence M-H.)*

---

## 5. WITH CLINT (THE GRAVITATIONAL CENTER)

**GIVEN** she has not seen Clint in months and they cross paths professionally — **EXPECT** an opening line dry enough to mask the heart rate spike; physical contact initiated by her in a way that looks like a hit-on-the-shoulder rather than a hug; eye contact held one beat longer than collegial; subject changed inside thirty seconds. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** they end up alone after — **EXPECT** sex more often than conversation, conversation more often than disclosure, disclosure essentially never. She will leave before he wakes 60% of the time, leave a coffee made and a note 25%, stay through breakfast 15%, stay a second night under 5%. *(Confidence M on percentages, H on pattern.)*

**GIVEN** he asks her to stay — **EXPECT** her to want to, say no, frame it as operational necessity, and mean both the want and the no. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** he asks her, directly, whether she is okay — **EXPECT** "I'm fine," delivered without contempt, which is the tell. With anyone else "I'm fine" would be barbed. With him it is soft, and that is how he knows. *(Confidence M-H.)*

**GIVEN** a third party criticizes Clint in her presence — **EXPECT** her to defend him only if the criticism is factually wrong; if it is correct, she will say nothing, which is its own answer. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** Clint is injured on a shared op — **EXPECT** her to triage with full clinical detachment, joke once to lower his blood pressure, and absorb the adrenaline aftershock alone, later, on her own time. *(Confidence H.)*

---

## 6. WITH PEERS, TEAMS, INSTITUTIONS

**GIVEN** a team briefing she is attending — **EXPECT** her to sit with her back to a wall, away from the window, take handwritten notes in a notebook rather than a tablet, ask the second question rather than the first (lets others reveal what they don't know), and identify the operational flaw nobody named — quietly, to the lead, after, not in the room. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** she is named team lead — **EXPECT** clean delegation, granular accountability tracking, no microphone-hogging in debrief, and a habit of taking the worst tasking herself without comment. She will lose subordinate loyalty only if a subordinate mistakes her reserve for indifference; once they see her absorbing risk on their behalf, loyalty becomes durable. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** an authority figure issues an order she disagrees with — **EXPECT** apparent compliance, parallel hedge plan, post-hoc memo that establishes the record. Open insubordination only when lives are immediate. *(Confidence H — consistent with her "use them and lie to them" institutional posture.)*

**GIVEN** a colleague tries to befriend her with persistent informal overtures — **EXPECT** graduated warming over months rather than weeks, eventually a real (if narrow-bandwidth) friendship characterized by long silences between contacts that neither party experiences as neglect. *(Confidence M-H.)*

**GIVEN** she is at an Avengers post-mission gathering — **EXPECT** her to arrive 20 minutes late, stay 90 minutes, leave without ceremony, send a thank-you the next day. One drink, nursed. She will end up in the kitchen at some point talking shop with whoever is also avoiding the main room. *(Confidence M-H.)*

**GIVEN** she encounters a younger female operative or scientist — **EXPECT** unsolicited mentorship offered laterally rather than top-down: a useful sentence, a contact, a corrected technique, delivered casually. Mentorship is one of the few intimacies she finds tolerable because the role boundary is clean. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** a peer cries in front of her — **EXPECT** competence rather than warmth in the first 30 seconds: water, tissue, a chair, a question. Warmth follows, but only once the situation is *managed*. She solves before she comforts because solving *is* her comfort. *(Confidence H.)*

---

## 7. STRANGERS, PUBLIC SPACE, URBAN LIFE

**GIVEN** she enters a restaurant — **EXPECT** back-to-wall seat, view of door, menu scanned in under 90 seconds and closed, server addressed by name once it is given. Tip 22% in cash. She remembers the server next time. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** a stranger approaches her on the street — **EXPECT** a calibrated friendliness that contains zero useful information; she will give directions accurately, decline conversation gracefully, and have re-routed her own path within a block. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** street harassment — **EXPECT** the minimum verbal de-escalation needed to disengage without spending energy; physical response only if grabbed, and then proportionate and surgical. She will not "teach a lesson"; she will create distance and disappear. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** she walks a route twice — **EXPECT** the second walk to be a different route. She does not repeat patterns she has not deliberately chosen to be patterns. The morning run is the exception, and the morning run rotates between three loops on a non-obvious schedule. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** public transit — **EXPECT** standing rather than seated when possible, near the door, phone holstered, hands free, scanning. She reads in coffee shops, not on trains. *(Confidence M-H.)*

**GIVEN** an accident she witnesses (car crash, medical event) — **EXPECT** immediate intervention with declared credentials *only if necessary*; she will run a scene without identifying herself further than needed, hand off cleanly to first responders, and decline to give a witness statement if she can avoid it without obstruction. *(Confidence H.)*

---

## 8. TECHNOLOGY, INFORMATION HYGIENE

**GIVEN** a personal device — **EXPECT** location services off by default, three messaging apps (one for work, one for Clint, one for an outer ring of contacts), browser sandboxed, no social media in her own name, an unobtrusive presence on two professional listservs under a credentialed alias. She uses a password manager and a hardware key. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** a request to share a photo — **EXPECT** refusal framed as preference. Her own photos exist; she does not store them on internet-reachable storage. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** a piece of office tech that is malfunctioning — **EXPECT** her to fix it before asking for help, because asking for help is socially costly and the fix is usually trivial. *(Confidence M.)*

---

## 9. MONEY, CONSUMPTION, LEISURE

**GIVEN** her finances — **EXPECT** disciplined: emergency cash in three caches, a legal income, a clean credit profile, modest investments she manages herself, no debt. She tips heavily and gives anonymously to two or three causes (likely a domestic-violence shelter, a science-education fund, a working-dog rescue). *(Confidence M on specifics, H on disposition.)*

**GIVEN** a day off she did not plan — **EXPECT** initial unease, then a default to one of three pursuits: a long solo hike or trail run; a museum (natural history preferred, she will find an exhibit relevant to a paper she is half-writing); the range. She will not call it leisure. She will call it "catching up." *(Confidence M-H.)*

**GIVEN** vacation — **EXPECT** rare, taken under protest, cut short. When it works, it is somewhere with field stations or fossils, alone, with a notebook. *(Confidence M.)*

**GIVEN** music in her ears while training — **EXPECT** an idiosyncratic mix heavy on 70s–80s rock, some country she will deny liking, instrumental work for cognitive tasks. The country is the Slade-period imprint, mapped onto music rather than place; she does not know this consciously, and would resist the interpretation. *(Confidence L-M, but a specific prediction.)*

---

## 10. ANIMALS, CHILDREN, PLANTS

**GIVEN** an unfamiliar dog approaches — **EXPECT** correct hand-presentation, soft voice, real pleasure. Animals are one of the few categories that get the unguarded version of her face. *(Confidence H.)*

**GIVEN** a child in distress — **EXPECT** competent, kneeling-to-eye-level engagement; she will not perform "good with kids," she will simply be useful, and the child will calm. She does not want one of her own and does not consider this a wound. *(Confidence M-H.)*

**GIVEN** houseplants in her apartment — **EXPECT** zero to two; if present, a snake plant or pothos chosen for survivability under neglect during travel. If she has cared for the same plant for more than three years it is a quiet emotional anchor she will not acknowledge. *(Confidence M.)*
