**(d) What is her relationship to the scientific identity?** The 1971 introduction frames her as a biologist; every subsequent decade has narrated her as an operative who happens to hold a doctorate. The *unintegrated scientific self* is a quiet asset on her ledger: a domain in which she has competence, satisfaction, and no trauma history. Whether she returns to substantive research — even part-time, even as a consultant — is one of the more underrated leverage points in her trajectory. Bench work would give her an arena where the demands are intellectual rather than ethical, where she does not have to absorb anyone's death, and where her compartmentalization is *adaptive* rather than pathological. The probability that she pursues this without prompting is moderate; with prompting from a credible source (a former dissertation advisor still living, an academic colleague, a research institute extending an invitation), it rises considerably.

**(e) The Slade memory, and the question of its disclosure.** She has now lived for decades with a private moral ledger entry that exactly one person (the dead man's brother, and certain readers of the Englehart run) knows in full. The question is whether she ever speaks it aloud, on her own initiative, to someone she has chosen. The answer determines whether the wound continues to run the operation or is finally retired to history. Predicted probability of voluntary disclosure within the next ten years: ~20%, conditional on the presence of a person who has earned that level of trust *and* who she believes can hear it without requiring her to manage their reaction. Barton is structurally disqualified — too much history, too much stake. A mentor figure or, more likely, a therapist she eventually accepts, is the realistic candidate.

---

### 6.4 Fork Points

These are the decision nodes where small inputs produce large divergences in trajectory.

**Fork 1 — The Next Captivity-Class Event.** Any prolonged loss-of-agency event (capture, possession, mind control, extended undercover assignment with identity submersion). *Growth branch*: she debriefs honestly, accepts structured psychological support, integrates the experience into the existing Skrull narrative as a *second instance* rather than a discrete event, which paradoxically makes both more tractable. *Catastrophe branch*: she walks out of the debrief on schedule, reports nothing, returns to duty within seventy-two hours, and the cumulative dissociative load crosses a threshold from which her current defenses cannot recover. Tell: how long she spends alone in the first month after extraction. More than two weeks of voluntary isolation is the warning sign.

**Fork 2 — A Protégée's Crisis.** When (not if) someone she has mentored makes a Slade-class unilateral decision of their own, possibly modeled consciously or unconsciously on hers. *Growth branch*: she recognizes the inheritance, treats the protégée's act as a mirror, and is forced into the disclosure she would never make for herself — she tells the protégée what it cost her, in order to stop them paying the same price. This is the single most likely route by which the Slade material reaches voluntary speech. *Catastrophe branch*: she covers for the protégée, replicates her own pattern at one remove, and confirms to herself that the lone-moral-actor template is not pathology but lineage.

**Fork 3 — Barton's Mortality or Hers.** A serious injury, terminal diagnosis, or near-death event affecting either party. *Growth branch*: forces the conversation that decades of operational tempo have permitted them to defer. Both have changed enough that the conversation could now be had. *Catastrophe branch*: she absorbs the event in her customary mode, executes whatever is required (caregiving, vengeance, both), and emerges further calcified. Note: she handled his apparent death in the 90s by becoming more, not less, herself. Repeat performance likely unless the surrounding social field actively scaffolds against it.

**Fork 4 — Institutional Realignment.** SHIELD has been dissolved, reconstituted, infiltrated, and replaced multiple times in her tenure. The next institutional rupture will force a choice: re-enlist under whatever banner replaces it, decline and free-lance, retire to academia, or build something of her own. *Growth branch*: she builds — a small, vetted unit, possibly intelligence-adjacent rather than paramilitary, organized around investigation rather than direct action, where her oversight prevents the institutional pathologies she has watched repeat. This gives her authorship over her professional environment for the first time. *Catastrophe branch*: she re-enlists by default, into an institution whose ethics she does not respect, and her quiet contempt for the chain of command produces a progressively larger gap between her stated mission and her actual operations. This is the path by which competent operators become rogue ones, and it is open to her.

**Fork 5 — The Body.** A medical event that the augmentation cannot route around — a hostile bio-agent, a Skrull-era latent injury surfacing, a piece of cellular damage the formulas accelerate rather than repair. *Growth branch*: forced convalescence she cannot tradecraft her way out of, which becomes (against her will) the longest sustained encounter with her own interior life she has had since the Skrull captivity. *Catastrophe branch*: she conceals symptoms, self-treats, and presents only when the condition is critical, at which point options are narrow and outcomes worse.

---

### 6.5 What Pushes Toward Growth

Specificity matters here, because vague prescriptions ("she should open up") will be defeated by her defenses in under a minute of contact.

- **Asymmetric relational structures**: mentorship, teaching, advisory roles. These channels permit warmth without requiring reciprocity she cannot supply. Maximize her exposure to these.
- **A therapist she selects herself, with security clearance, who is willing to be *useful* before being *deep*.** She will not tolerate a clinician who leads with feelings. She will tolerate one who leads with operational consultation — sleep, performance, decision-making under uncertainty — and lets the deeper material surface on her timeline. Three to five years of this is the realistic envelope for substantive movement.
- **Re-engagement with science as identity, not as cover.** Lab time. Publication. Conference attendance. The restoration of a domain where her competence is non-lethal.
- **A peer who shares the augmentation/aging asymmetry** and is willing to discuss it without dramatizing it. Conversion of an existential alienation into a cohort experience is structurally protective.
- **One disclosure, voluntary, of the Slade material to one chosen person.** Not therapy-extracted, not crisis-forced — chosen. This is the single act with the highest leverage in her file. Every other defense reorganizes around it.
- **Permission, explicitly granted by someone she respects, to be the rescued rather than the rescuer in a specific bounded instance.** She will refuse it the first dozen times. The thirteenth time, under sufficient exhaustion, she may accept. The acceptance is the data point that recodes the self-concept.

---

### 6.6 What Pushes Toward Catastrophe

- **Reinforcement of the lone-moral-actor template by operational success.** Every Slade-class decision that produces a good outcome strengthens the template. The system rewards her for the behavior that is killing her interior life. Counter-pressure must come from people, since outcomes will not provide it.
- **A second impersonation event of any kind.** Probability over a ten-year window is non-trivial given her threat environment. Without prior integration of the first, the second is destabilizing in ways her current defenses are not built for.
- **Loss of Barton without prior reconciliation of the relational ledger.** Unfinished business with the primary attachment figure, with no possibility of finishing it, is a known driver of complicated grief and chronic dysthymia. The window for the conversation is *now*, not later, and she is the one who has to open it.
- **Institutional capture by an organization whose ethics she does not respect.** Produces the slow corruption pathway: small accommodations, private contempt, escalating unilaterality, eventual rupture in which she is cast as the villain by the institution she was carrying. She is vulnerable to this because her loyalty is to people and outcomes, not banners, and the institution will not understand the distinction until she has broken with it publicly.
- **A protégée's death she could plausibly have prevented.** The guilt structure she already carries will not absorb this without significant decompensation. She has not been tested at this load. Prediction: she does not survive it intact, in any meaningful psychological sense, without prior therapeutic infrastructure already in place.
- **Forced disclosure of the Slade material by a third party** — leaked, retconned-public, weaponized in an operational context. Removes her authorship of the narrative, which is the one thing she has preserved. Recovery from this is possible but slow and will require the relational support she has spent her life refusing to build.

---

### 6.7 Net Assessment

Subject is, at present, *durably functional and quietly unreachable*. She will continue to be an exceptional operator, a demanding mentor, a difficult intimate, and a private carrier of unprocessed material that periodically asserts itself through unilateral action. The trajectory is not toward dramatic collapse; her defenses are too robust and too well-rehearsed for that. The trajectory is toward a slow, dignified, competent isolation that she will narrate to herself as freedom and that her file will record as the long-form expression of the wound she has been managing since 1971.

The growth path exists and is specifiable. It requires three things she has historically refused: a chosen confidant, a clinical relationship, and one voluntary disclosure. Each of these is improbable in isolation; in combination, transformative. The probability that all three occur within the next decade absent a forcing event is low — call it 10–15%. With one forcing event (Fork 2 or Fork 5 are the most likely catalysts), it rises to perhaps 40%. With two, considerably higher.

She is, in the end, recoverable. She has not made herself unrecoverable, which itself is significant given the trauma load — the ethical and relational core is intact, the empathy is rationed but real, the capacity for change exists in latent form. What she lacks is not the material for repair but the permission, which she will not grant herself and must therefore receive from outside.

The file should be re-reviewed at any Fork-class event, and annually regardless. Subject's stability is real and her drift is also real, and the distance between the two is exactly the work of attention this dossier exists to perform.

## Relationship Graph
### [[Clinton Francis Barton (Hawkeye (also: Ronin, Goliath - briefly, Golden Archer - briefly))]]
- Twice-married, twice-divorced. The central relational fact of her life and the one she can't fully close out.
- Complementary asymmetry: she plans, he improvises. She offers it as contribution; he reads it as control.
- Failure mode: concealment in either direction (her on Slade, him on operational secrets) detonates the bond. A third strike would not be recoverable.
- Leverage: a credible threat to Clint reaches her past every defense she has; conversely, his praise is a currency she pretends not to count.

### [[Jessica Drew (Spider-Woman)]]
- Closest peer bond. Low-friction, mutually competent, no gendered scripts.
- Failure mode: a Skrull-imposture-style identity violation between them would be catastrophic precisely because the trust is foundational.
- Leverage: Jessica is one of the few people whose call she answers immediately.

### [[Natasha Romanoff (Black Widow)]]
- Professional respect at peer altitude. Tradecraft trust, intimacy reserved.
- Failure mode: an op where Natasha plays her without telling her would route through the Slade wound.
- Leverage: Natasha can ask her to do things no one else can ask her to do, and Bobbi will weigh it seriously.

### [[Nicholas Joseph Fury (Nick Fury)]]
- Original handler. The institution she grew up inside, personified. She trusts him operationally and audits him constantly.
- Failure mode: a Fury op that uses her body or biochemistry without consent (cf. the serum administration) would be a line.
- Leverage: institutional appeals routed through Fury have weight she would deny giving them.

### Lincoln Slade Phantom Rider
- Dead. Index trauma. The wound that defines her ethical interior.
- Failure mode: any resurrection, descendant, or mystical echo of Slade is a structural emergency - the one stimulus that bypasses her mastery defense entirely.
- Leverage: an adversary who reconstructs the Slade scenario controls a panic response she otherwise does not have.

### Lance Hunter
- Intimacy without re-entanglement. Adult, bounded, mutually authored.
- Failure mode: if he tries to upgrade it to a Clint-class bond, she exits.
- Leverage: low - she has structured the relationship to minimize it.

### Wca Staff And Mentees
- Her bench. Her institution. Her standards.
- Failure mode: internal corruption - which she will excise without warning the corrupted party.
- Leverage: threatening her people gets a cold, decisive response no negotiator can soften.

### Skrull Empire
- The collective adversary that took years from her. Never personalized into a single figure, which is part of the wound.
- Failure mode: dormant rage that could be activated by any sufficiently large betrayal-trauma echo.
- Leverage: invoking Skrull tradecraft (impersonation, infiltration) hits a vigilance circuit she will run hot until resolved.
